                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 台灣貓奴在美國
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 貓奴版禁談宗教政治，以喵星人的幸福為宗旨研究健康飲食健康生活與有貓的快樂人生，共同創造貓奴與貓星人的幸福人生。 ★本版不歡迎貓狗販子，更禁止提供寵物販賣資訊與鼓吹野生動物飼養相關文章。不鼓勵品種迷思，請領養代替購買。認知不同請自行退出。★ ★如有明顯錯誤觀念影片文章，管理員會即時刪除並說明以免誤導大眾★ ★開放買賣/徵求/交換/贈送寵物用品，不允許商家營利po文。本版只提供交易平台, 並不干涉金錢交易的行為，如有糾紛請私下解決。★ ★本版開放個人創作者替手作商品作推廣。前提是有跟版友互動的人（不是專po廣告文），不是純營利量產商家。★ ★本版禁止只張貼內容農場連結卻不互動的版友。累犯兩次以上將不通知移除+封鎖。 內容農場是什麼：https://www.facebook.com/groups/taiwanesecatlovers/permalink/578534062295347/ ★禁止張貼藏有賺回饋金的商場連結，例如：Amazon associates program。初犯會勸導，累犯會刪除貼文不另行通知。★ ★如有違反版規者，發文不備份刪除。好生事鬧事、針對人身攻擊謾罵、負面情緒的正義魔人、或挑戰公理是非、並跟管理員起糾紛者！一律不討論並直接踢出社團並封鎖。封鎖管理員者必踢，被管理員個人封鎖的，是管理員佛心沒把私人恩怨公器私用請安分。★ ★若轉貼文內容不當，或涉及錯誤養貓觀念，板主得刪除並公告。★ ★發文請盡量以繁體中文、書面語或英文為主，以便板友閱讀。★ ★若有較為血腥的照片、影片，請將放至留言處，並在本文加註警語。★ 關於貓食問題，檔案區有資料跟貓食排行。如何找檔案區： https://www.facebook.com/groups/taiwanesecatlovers/permalink/579289702219783/ 【貓奴互助會】 （經版友建議製作居住城市清單，好方便成立互助會，出門旅遊能互相照應家裡貓主子） 原post: https://www.facebook.com/groups/taiwanesecatlovers/permalink/523827151099372/ Google Drive表單請自行填寫： https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1xyiEpXXbfDppXO01C49GajCsWpHlhlr1--vrK5wT-H8/edit?usp=sharing 管理員： ●Angie Hu ●Chole Tsai 康樂股長： ●Jill S. 【送養跟幫喵喵找家】 由於本團是closed group，在團裡開的相簿跟上傳的照片無法分享到其他地方，所以送養文的貓咪照請先在自己的版上開好相簿，設公開（Public）再用share的功能分享到社團裡。 設公開相簿教學： https://www.facebook.com/groups/taiwanesecatlovers/permalink/507795779369176/ ★送養文請附上 ●貓咪照片 ●送養原因 ●貓咪性別 ●貓咪年紀（大概也可以） ●有無結紮（optional） ●預防針施打狀況 ●貓咪所在地（&lt;---最重要，因為本團有來自各州的貓奴） ●聯絡方式 ★買賣發文請附上： ●物品照片 ●物品名稱 ●物品狀況 ●物品所在地 ●價錢與運費 ●交易方式（面交或郵寄） ●取貨地點（如果是面交物品的話） ※ 免責聲明 ※ 「台灣貓奴在美國」只提供平台，不收取任何佣金。 不擁有任何版友分享的文章，圖片之版權。 不對會員提供的商品資料做任何擔保。 不對會員提供訊息的正確性或完整性做任何擔保。 不對會員物品買賣所得做任何擔保。 如買賣引起任何法律糾紛，請自行承擔責任。
                </div>

                 🐶🐱🐎🐷Welcome to pit bulls and friends group , this group is all about positive postings awarness and responsible owners who can showcase their beautiful dogs not only for pit bulls, but all dog breeds welcomed, Pics are welcomed, question posts , advice, rehoming, lost found dogs and for adopting/rehomed by law pups have to be at least 8 weeks above .. Dogs should be fixed before being rehomed or if not fixed we can help find a way to get them fixed for u before getting into a home....or find a Reputable rescue. Rehoming fees can not be an outrageous amount and please add location, utd, age, contact info, good with other dogs, cats, kids... etc if not 🛇 it will be removed...that also goes for reposted pics from other groups, please make sure u are in contact with o.p (original poster) When posting for donations please ☚ post further info on whats going on and proof ✔ Graphic videos like a person killing a dog will be removed ,any other pics or videos that maybe graphic, please post a warning... ⚠ other than that u can share great personal, photos, videos ,live videos or stories if u have any 😁💙 What wont be tolerated is ....☚😒 Disrespect towards anyone. .. This group is not a group where u can Advertise your dog for breeding, No back yard breeding or any kind of breeding, there is groups already made for that... No selling your litters,or puppy , no puppy flippers this group isn't like animals lovers, pets forless , buy sell groups or for sale .... ●No cross posting pics of puppies from groups ,if u do please cut off name and group before posting asking for help or u have a plan in place, like... rescue them, or calling on ac to report them , ( no animal control won't take and kill them, they will fine them and document, investigate and then go from there) if ur going to do something do it, if not u are giving them advertisement and that isn't allowed on the group and will be removed and will lead to the memeber being removed if it keeps happening, ●No asking for medical advice , dont want anyone to be blamed for something that made your pet even worse , please go to a vet , where they can properly diagnosis your dog, Before its to late ●Please ask us before posting up another group , if it's a sell group it will be removed, ●Please stay on top of your posts✔ double posts will be removed ... ● Grapic videos or pics maybe posted but must have a warning, no need to report them if there is already one, this is an awarness , group also .. ● No talking about dogs ears cropped and flopped allowed ● please ask admins before posting your group.. 🐶This group is all about unity and a place where we can be proud to show off our dogs, anyone who dont follow will be warned, deleted off the group, thank u and enjoy 💙 Please add anyone u know who would enjoy the fun 😀 Any questions or comments, concerns please tag or pm us Admins are Roxanne corralejo Jessica lety Frances Le Blanc Ana p .c

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ACTION AGAINST ANIMAL ABUSE (4A) Welcome to 4A - Protect Our Wildlife (and Endangered Species) (4A-POW) This 4A group is concerned with the protection of all wild land mammals and birds, particularly those which are poached, hunted, or both, and especially those whose populations have become drastically reduced as a result of hunting, poachers, or any other reason. Ocean and sea creatures and sea birds are covered in our Protect Marine Life group at www.facebook.com/groups/4A.PML . Please feel free to add any of your animal loving friends who want to help protect our land wildlife and endangered species. If you have been added to this group and do not wish to be in it please accept our apologies and simply click the 'Leave Group' button. For a list with links to all 4A groups please visit our website page www.ActionAgainstAnimalAbuse.com/Invite

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  Welcome to T.R.E. We are an OPEN MINDED group that accepts many different methods and approaches to husbandry. If you are not able to play nice, do not join. This is your one stop shop for all things REPTILE related. (This includes feeders) We also accept Amphibians &amp; Arachnids. Ask questions, share photos, and give sound advice on reptile husbandry. This is a POSITIVE place. We will NOT tolerate any verbal abuse or mockery. Sarcasm and a sense of humor is greatly appreciated, however: If you have a problem with a group member, please contact an admin. Please do not go back and forth on posts. We all have the same goal in mind; to provide exceptional care for our reptiles. Let's all come together as a community to spread awareness and show the world the joy these reptiles can bring!! Every Wednesday (whatever Wednesday) we allow members to make ONE POST unrelated to reptiles. You MUST put a warning on ALL live/thaw feeding videos or they will be removed. You MUST also put a warning on Live Feed photos and post them in the comments under your warning. We do NOT allow Gofundme's. No questions asked. You get ONE warning before you are removed from the group permanently. Debates about reptile love or emotions are no longer allowed due to the consistent drama and arguments that arise from them. Any posts or comments trying to start a debate on this subject will be removed. Please no Religious, Political or Racial posts. While you can block other members, you cannot block admins. Doing so will result in you being immediately removed from the group!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 南加州寵物俱樂部
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 管理員公告 加入社團的朋友請先看貼文遵守貼文規定和版規，違反者直接刪文或是刪除團員資格不會另外通知，也不要私訊管理員詢問原因 ♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️ ➡️在社團貼「領養文」需要註明 領養費（免費也要註明），目前被領養寵物的所在地（州，城市，海外需註明國家）和聯絡方式（私訊，電話，或是其他聯絡方式），沒有提供以上三點，貼文不會被批准 ➡️ 所有「lost and found pet的貼文」請一定要註明牠們被撿到或是走失的地點（城市），也請用「英文」張貼或是轉貼在社團內，方便其他團員在短時間分享去其他社團，沒有註明「地點」的貼文不會被批准 ➡️諮詢寵物獸醫推薦，寵物美容，寵物出國或入境（打針）這類的貼文，請附上座標（你目前的城市），方便團員幫忙 ♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️♦️ #版規 （1）這裡提供給寵物迷一個分享平台，大家互相交流照顧寵物的知識經驗和生活點滴，在社團發言請互相尊重，不允許不禮貌挑釁或是泛政治宗教的貼文和留言，請在提問和發言時不要忘記說「請；謝謝；和對不起」，喜歡的貼文也請按個讚，增加團員之間良好互動 （2）請勿封鎖管理員，一經發現立刻刪除團員資格，不另外通知 （3）管理員有權力刪除任何讓人不舒服和有爭議的貼文或是留言，刪除不會另外通知和解釋 （4）社團禁止隨意張貼團員個人連結，例如本團團員個人的社團，粉絲頁和網站 （5）團員貼文之後，不可隨意刪除貼文和留言，版內貼文，照片與留言內容截圖分享時，請注意隱私，人名或是個資要反白 （6）對自己不認同的貼文和留言，請尊重對方，盡量做到不看不發言繞道而行，社團的每個人都有發文發言權，但最終裁決權由管理員決定 （7）禁止所有募款和義賣活動，社團大型版聚需先經過管理員批准 （8）禁止在社團內貼文找貓狗（或是其他寵物）配種，禁止上傳殘忍虐待動物和敗壞社會風氣的影片和內容，禁止任何買賣寵物的貼文 （9）全新和二手寵物用品想販售，貼文前先私訊管理員，amazon寵物特價商品可以從其他link轉貼分享，但是不歡迎商家在社團內找團員免費試用寫心得或是直接貼連結賺錢 （10）寵物有任何問題，請先來社團詢問或是打電話問獸醫，請不要沒有經過社團詢問直接私訊管理員 （11）詢問問題之前，請先用放大鏡🔍加「關鍵字」在社團內先搜尋之前舊文，社團內有非常豐富的資訊可以參考 （12）管理員不會24小時在線上，如果有看到與社團不符的貼文，留言或是買賣廣告文，請按檢舉通知我們，我們會刪文刪留言和移除發文的團友 [備註] 撿到貓狗小動物該如何處理？ 先照像貼文發社群，帶去掃晶片，沒有晶片就直接送去撿到地區的官方shelter 本社團希望撿到毛小孩的團友，第一件事不是上社團來找人領養牠們，而是可以負責任先帶牠們去掃晶片和做好flyer去撿到地點附近和上傳社群貼文，如果你做不到這些最基本的，請送牠們去撿到地區的官方收容所，請不要自行留著送養，牠們也許是有主人，牠們的主人也許正在著急心碎💔尋找牠們，寵物主人並不知道如何聯絡到你，但是寵物主人一定先去家附近的官方收容所尋找牠們

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Freshwater Aquarium Help and Support Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a help and support group aimed at sharing and problem solving all things freshwater aquatics. We all enjoy this diverse hobby and need insight, guidance, and help at times to succeed. Being a large group we have the benefit of a wealth of experience and knowledge, which you are encouraged to share. When requesting support or advice, be aware that additional information will likely be required. Healthy aquariums require an array of well maintained and tuned parameters. Disruption or imbalance to any of these may cause ill effect and a consideration of multiple factors will likely be required to resolve your problem. If you do post, please follow-up. Do you best to respond to additional questions and communicate with those who would help. Likewise, when responding to a post, or providing support, please see the issue through. Respond to questions and provide your insights to the best of your ability and please, to avoid misinformation, do not respond to questions you are unsure about answering. To make sure that others can effectively help you with whatever issue you are having with your tank, please provide us with some basic information. ie: Aquarium size, Nitrates, Ammonia, Nitrites, PH, KH/GH (if you have the test available), Temp. If you are having plant issues, please also include your photoperiod (time your lights are on) If you dose fertilizer, what types, quantities, and how often. Lastly, are you using injected C02. This information will help others help you. Also, "FINE" isn't a measurement 😁
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">1.3&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">22 篇新帖</span></span>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Endangered Species and Animals Under Threat
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for animal that are threatened in the wild. Evolutionarily Distinct and Globally Endangered (EDGE) species have few close relatives and are often extremely distinct in the way they look, live and behave. These unique species are also on the verge of extinction, and if they disappear there will be nothing like them left on the planet. Some EDGE species, such as elephants and pandas are well known, but others, such as the Yangtze River dolphin (the world's rarest cetacean), Gardiner’s Seychelles frog (possibly the world’s smallest amphibian) and the egg-laying long-beaked echidnas, remain poorly understood. Alarmingly, two-thirds of the top 100 EDGE mammal species are currently receiving little or no conservation attention. The situation is even more worrying for amphibians, with 85% of the top 100 amphibians are currently receiving little or no conservation attention. The EDGE of Existence programme aims to address this conservation gap by raising awareness of these species, identifying the dominant threat processes affecting them, and implementing conservation strategies for a number of Focal species each year. The Species section of the website provides information on the top 100 EDGE mammals and amphibians, poorly-known (or potential) EDGE species, and the ten most Evolutionarily Distinct species in each group. Visit the search page to look for a specific species, or scroll through the lists and learn more about the weird and wonderful species we are highlighting. Info through the page of: http://www.edgeofexistence.org/ 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 * NO NON-HORSE RELATED POSTS* Rules are Simple: No Non-Horse Related Posts - Discussions or Sales (**Realtors, you may only Post HORSE PROPERTY and it must state that It Is, in the property description.) No Disrespectful Comments or Posts (There are Other Forums for that.) ___________________________________ If you wish to Invite Friends to Join this Group, Please send them the Link, as they do not see The Questions they have to answer to join. _____________________________________ I hope all Members will help grow and enjoy making this a great Horse Community Site, with posting's of Events, Shows - English-Western-Barrel Racing, Playday's, Clinics, Clubs (if you are an ETI Member post ETI Corral # and Area and any Info on Poker Rides, etc.), Horse Rescues, Trainers, Farriers, Vets, Horse Dentist's, Equine Massage Therapists,Horse Photographers, Horse Transporters and All Horse Related Businesses and Services, Jobs and Jobs Wanted that are horse related. Sales of horses, tack, pickup trucks for hauling horse trailers, horse trailers, hay, horse housing and any items pertaining to horses or a horsey way of life. I would also like to see this site as an open platform for all horse related questions where others that may have an answer may share their knowledge or impart info on training, feed, health, best places to trail ride, best feed and tack stores in your area's and since we are a Horse Community, please feel free to post pic's of your horses, trail ride pics, show pic's. Above all else please enjoy Your Site.

(This is a Facebook rule, which the Admins and Mods are protesting. We do believe these posts in our group and other FB groups are beneficial.) · Rude, offensive, bullying or disturbing posts or comments, including photos of deceased birds, are unacceptable. · You may not ban Administrators or Moderators or make your posts invisible to us. It will be assumed that you intend to break one or more of our rules and act accordingly. We invite all members to post information, photos and especially photos. Welcome!                  Welcome to I Love Cats group! This is a place to share our love of cats of all kinds. RULES 1. This is an international group, so write English please. 2. If anyone has a problem about someone else's post, please contact the Admin about the issue and they will work out the problem to their best judgment. 4. Please no Gofundme posts allowed. 10. Please do not post political opinions. 11.               <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Venomous Reptiles
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Venomous Reptiles! This group is for the discussion of the many aspects of the venomous reptile hobby including, but not limited to, husbandry, handling, &amp; field herping. The goal is to promote the conservation &amp; responsible keeping of venomous reptiles through education &amp; guidance. Please keep discussions limited to the following families/genera: Ahaetulla, Atractaspidae, Boiga, Dispholidus, Elapidae, Heloderma, Hydrodynastes, Macropisthodon, Rhabdophis, Rhamnophis, Telescopus, Thelotornis, Thrasops, &amp; Viperidae. This list of approved families/genera is subject to change at any time at the admins' discretion. Please refrain from posting any "For Sale" &amp; "Wanted" posts. Please use the "Venomous reptile classifieds" group for that purpose (https://www.facebook.com/groups/360560250675015/). Feel free to post any venomous reptile-related pictures &amp; videos, too. You can even make an album to share your collection. Please do not spam the group with multiple pictures at once; just make an album in the group &amp; post the album. Please do not post any free-handling pictures. This group will be kept on the "Closed" setting in order to keep out any of the hobby's enemies, so feel free to discuss some of the touchier subjects of the hobby provided that you adhere to the group rules in doing so. Feel free to add any fellow venomous keepers &amp; enthusiasts as well. Please refrain from the use of harsh language &amp; try to keep all posts respectful. Trolling will not be tolerated. Absolutely no illegal activity will be tolerated. Admins: Brandon Havro, John Zegel, Devin Maus, Josh Lamia, William Drake, Sladen Slayden, Hasse Bergman, Devin Moyer, Morton Brown, &amp; Christopher Hyatt.
                </div>

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! This is a support community for the page: https://www.facebook.com/LAAdoptDogs/ This group is for the community to share useful info and content related to dog life, dog ownership, dog lovers, and dog adoptions! To combat spam, scams, and unwanted clutter, all posts and posters must be approved first! NOTICE: IF YOU ARE ADOPTING OUT OR REHOMING DOGS: FIRST post your ad(s) to our page: https://www.facebook.com/LAAdoptDogs/ Post your ad(s) to the community section on our page so that they can be verified and approved. Once approved, your ads will automatically disseminate across our network! ---------------------------------------- We love dogs and we're happy you're here. If you wish to be a member please follow these rules. Group Rules: #1 If you are posting a dog for adoption or rehoming: - You must have valid profile credentials to be approved. Details such as location (city/state), friends list, and some basic profile information should be visible so that viewers can evaluate your authenticity. - YOU MUST submit your ad(s) to our Facebook Page: https://www.facebook.com/LAAdoptDogs/community to be vetted and approved. (Once approved, your ad(s) will disseminate across our network.) #2 Dog Post Guidelines: If you are posting a dog for adoption or rehoming, please include the following: - Clear, tasteful pictures of the pet (no text on the pictures, phone numbers or contact info) - Location, gender, age, breed and pertinent background info - Adoption or rehoming information and costs - Contact Information #3 If you are a member of this group: - No Negative/Hate Speech or Bullying. Be friendly and courteous. #4 If you are posting in this group: - Do not submit posts IN SEARCH OF... a dog or any particular feature (breed, gender, age...etc)... browse our pages and website instead! - Please keep posts related to dog life, dog ownership, dog lovers, and dog adoptions! Posts about lost dogs are allowed! - No Promotions or Spam. Self promotion or irrelevant links are not allowed. Keep posts content driven. - All posts must be approved first - only useful information that is helpful to the community will be permitted! #5 If you are adopting pets: - Make sure to exercise due diligence and investigate the person you’re dealing with - Report puppy mills, illegal, or inhumane behavior - Don’t electronically send money to people you do not know or have not met. Deal with people in person for safety. - No one is responsible for your safety or actions but you. This is an organic and natural community and you alone are responsible for protecting yourself and ensuring you don’t get scammed. Exercise due diligence with everyone you deal with. #6 We are in this together, to create a welcoming environment. Give more to the group than you take. Be Kind and Courteous. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. If you see violations to the rules please report them to the moderators.

                 This group is a place for cowboys / cowgirls, ranch / farm folks and horse lovers to relax, have fun and make friends. Feel free to share your stories, experiences and pictures (as long as they are clean). No selfies will be allowed unless they are cowboy / country related. Please read all the rules before you send posts and pics for approval. 1) NO SELFIES ~ This is not a dating site. Any picture that makes you look like you are looking for attention, a date or hook up will be deleted. 2) NO ADVERTISING ~ Unless it's for Rodeo or other horse events, any form of advertising will be declined. 3) NO POLITICS ~ All political posts will be taken down and the members will be immediately blocked from the group without warning or second chances. 4) NO DISRESPECT ~ Disrespect towards any member, myself or any of my moderators will not be tolerated. Any disrespectful or rude comments will be deleted and those group members will also be banned without warning. If you have a problem with a group member, please in box me, Marie-Anne Morrissette or one of my moderators about your issue and we will take care of it. 5) NO DRAMA ~ Those of you who choose to entertain drama in a post will be banned from the group. 6) NO WATCH PARTIES 7) NO FUNDRAISERS 8) NO CHAIN MAIL 9) POSTS COMPLAINING ABOUT OTHER MEMBERS AND / OR ADMINS / MODERATORS WILL NOT BE APPROVED. ALL COMPLAINTS MUST BE DEALT WITH PRIVATELY. 10) NO BLOCKING OF ANY ADMIN OR MODERATOR ~ Blocking an admin or moderator will get you automatically and permanently banned from The Cowboy Way. As a member of The Cowboy Way, if you see anything offensive or that goes against the group rules, please report it and / or inbox me or one of my moderators about it. You cooperation is important in order to keep this group fun and safe for everyone. If you have a problem with another member and / or their posts, you can block them but blocking me or my moderators is not permitted and doing so will get you banned from the group. Kick back and relax and don't forget to add your friends. Thank y'all and have fun ! ~ Classy Cowgirl ~

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 PARROT STATION
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group was created by parrot YouTuber and Vlogger Marlene Mc’Cohen so that she could meet her YouTube fans and fellow parrot lovers!! This is a friendly, parrot educational group for all parrot lovers to share parrot stories and help each other with parrot questions. You are responsible to know the rules of this group. Please read them. GROUP MEMBER RULES: 1. Please do not judge, attack, shame, or be rude to other members! Parronts are here to learn from each other and parrot owners will be scared to ask questions if they are attacked. Make everyone feel welcome. Every bird is a star here!! 2. NO CURSING OR FOUL LANGUAGE! This includes %%$# signs or symbols. Keep it classy! There are kids on his page so we have to have respect....and unfortunately that does go for the birds too. 3. No buying and selling of parrots or other items such as cages or toys. There are a lot of parrot selling scams, so whether you are legit or not, your posts will be deleted and you may be banned. 4. No GoFund me sites or asking for donations. Although I’m sure many of our members would love to help, it will ruin the experience if this page flooded with gofundme requests. 5. Do not promote your own YouTube or parrot training pages, books and/ or videos. This would be a conflict of interest as Parrot Station was created by YouTuber and Parrot Trainer, Marlene Mc’Cohen. 6. Please do NOT make your own albums on this page or add to them. Although it is easy to do accidentally, it clouds up album organization planned for the page and messes with the structure plans of the album you are adding to. 7. If your bird has passed we would love to honor your bird and his memory by adding his/her story to the REMEMBERED SOULS album. To do this, please choose your favorite picture of your parrot (1 picture) write your favorite story and his dates and contact the moderator in charge and they will add it for you, if they haven’t contacted you already :( 8. Our moderators feel like it is easier for them to manage posts when they are in English and as they are putting in massive amounts of work, I ask us all to respect their decision. 9. No Advertising! If you are interested in advertising opportunities, please contact admin Marlene Mc’Cohen. 10. Do not make any live videos, this is reserved for admin only. 11. No pictures of chicks. We are sorry but too many scammers are using pictures to try to sell their birds. 12. Posts that show the harming or potential harming of any parrot will be removed. 13. The moderators also reserve the right to remove any posts that they feel will cause arguments and are not helpful in parrot education. MODERATORS FOR THIS PAGE ARE: Shean Pao, Jill Smith, Niecey Belanger, Amy Beets-Peterson, Ali Wise, Alyssa M. Grasso, Stacey Jane Craft, Ken Cheatham, Raphael Sher, Rosalie Soussan, Alisa Rizzo, Neo Coyle, Jessica Burton, Dani Love, Ester De Jong, Nisa Rojas
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Birding California
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! Birding California is designed to allow new, as well as experienced birders to share sightings, pictures, videos, and thoughts and ideas, too! Though mostly photos are posted here we encourage group members to post anything related to WILD BIRDS IN CALIFORNIA. Field trips, conservation topics, interesting articles, trips reports, etc. are all permissible in the group. If you are a new member of the group PLEASE READ the guidelines on the pinned post on the main page of the group! Thanks! **POSTING RULES (please read these before making your first post to the group)** -When posting to the group, please include the NAME OF THE BIRD, LOCATION, and DATE with EACH PHOTO. If you do not know the ID of the bird, please state that you are asking for help. If it is a sensitive species that you don't want to give a specific location for (e.g., threatened species like Spotted Owl) just giving a very general location like "Humboldt County" is fine. - Need ID Help? If you can't figure out an ID, there are plenty of people here to help. Just include where and when the photo was taken and we'll do our best to help you work through the identification of the species. - Posts from California of FREE-FLYING WILD BIRDS (or rarities in neighboring states that California birders might want to attempt to see) ONLY. This means we don't want posts of domestic geese that live off a breadline in a local city park. OTHER GENERAL RULES TO FOLLOW (See the pinned post on the main page)

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! This is a support community for the page: https://www.facebook.com/SoCalAdoptDogs/ This group is for the community to share useful info and content related to dog life, dog ownership, dog lovers, and dog adoptions! To combat spam, scams, and unwanted clutter, all posts and posters must be approved first! NOTICE: IF YOU ARE ADOPTING OUT OR REHOMING DOGS: FIRST post your ad(s) to our page: https://www.facebook.com/SoCalAdoptDogs/ Post your ad(s) to the community section on our page so that they can be verified and approved. Once approved, your ads will automatically disseminate across our network! ---------------------------------------- We love dogs and we're happy you're here. If you wish to be a member please follow these rules. Group Rules: #1 If you are posting a dog for adoption or rehoming: - You must have valid profile credentials to be approved. Details such as location (city/state), friends list, and some basic profile information should be visible so that viewers can evaluate your authenticity. - YOU MUST submit your ad(s) to our Facebook Page: https://www.facebook.com/SoCalAdoptDogs/community to be vetted and approved. (Once approved, your ad(s) will disseminate across our network.) #2 Dog Post Guidelines: If you are posting a dog for adoption or rehoming, please include the following: - Clear, tasteful pictures of the pet (no text on the pictures, phone numbers or contact info) - Location, gender, age, breed and pertinent background info - Adoption or rehoming information and costs - Contact Information #3 If you are a member of this group: - No Negative/Hate Speech or Bullying. Be friendly and courteous. #4 If you are posting in this group: - Do not submit posts IN SEARCH OF... a dog or any particular feature (breed, gender, age...etc)... browse our pages and website instead! - Please keep posts related to dog life, dog ownership, dog lovers, and dog adoptions! Posts about lost dogs are allowed! - No Promotions or Spam. Self promotion or irrelevant links are not allowed. Keep posts content driven. - All posts must be approved first - only useful information that is helpful to the community will be permitted! #5 If you are adopting pets: - Make sure to exercise due diligence and investigate the person you’re dealing with - Report puppy mills, illegal, or inhumane behavior - Don’t electronically send money to people you do not know or have not met. Deal with people in person for safety. - No one is responsible for your safety or actions but you. This is an organic and natural community and you alone are responsible for protecting yourself and ensuring you don’t get scammed. Exercise due diligence with everyone you deal with. #6 We are in this together, to create a welcoming environment. Give more to the group than you take. Be Kind and Courteous. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. If you see violations to the rules please report them to the moderators.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hope For Paws website: http://www.hopeforpaws.org Flickr page http://www.flickr.com/eldad75 310 8801416 we re an ALL Animal Rescue in Los Angeles,CA 8950 west Olympic blvd no 525 Los Angeles CA 90211 We are on facebook hope for paws group hope for paws page eldad hagar extended profile page about us: A 501 c-3 nonprofit We rescue strays that nobody else can. Our animals suffer from being exposed to the elements for far too long. Broken bones, attacks from predators, parasites, all types of infections, starvation, dehydration: we get them the best medical care possible. Comfort and quality of life is our main concern. We only allow our animals to go to foster care after they are able to leave the hospital. No cages, no boarding. Finally they are adopted into loving permanent homes. We videotape as many rescues as we can in order to show the world the plight of animal homelessness and the need for spay/neuter and adoption. People from all parts of the globe have written to us that our videos have changed their perception of streetand shelter animals and as a result have chosen to adopt and treat these animalsthey once never gave thought to, with kindness and patience. Pets are family; an emotional and financial commitment for their entire life.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Baby Animals Make Everything Better
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ***If you do not answer the questions you will not be added to the group! PLEASE ANSWER ALL QUESTIONS!*** PLEASE READ BEFORE POSTING! Welcome to the group!! I created this group as a way for a couple of friends and I to send a way to brighten our friends' days. It grew and here we are! So now that we're a large group, let's set down some standards: - everyone is welcome to post! - While we know you love your furbabies, please only post them if they are in baby form! Grown up pets will probably be deleted. - note that only people who are IN the group can see things in the group, so rather than tagging a friend, invite them! - Please keep your posts to focusing on ONLY baby animals of the non-human variety, and do not post fully grown pets/animals or links to causes, products, advertisements or events unless they are an opportunity for me to pet puppies. - As an extension of the above, this is not a sale group, do not post your babies for sale here. Also spay and neuter your pets, everyone. - Be awesome to one another, people posting rude comments and starting fights will be removed. - People posting wildly inappropriate or offensive things will be removed without warning and blocked, as we will assume they are viruses or bots. If you got hacked and someone used your account to post these things and you were blocked, please send me a message to verify your real life human-ness. - Please do not post your own albums, we will delete them. - If multiple people post the same item in a relatively short period of time, I will delete all but the first one posted. Please do not be upset if your post is deleted, but if you are unsure of why it was, feel free to ask. If the above is not followed, we may have to remove your post, and that makes everyone unhappy, so make sure to follow the standards! However, we understand we're all animal lovers here, so please feel free to use the pinned post to post your furbabies in the comments! Admins: Ivy Lockhart Kenda Post Liz Reinhardt

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Aquarium Fish Help For Beginners
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 • No advertising allowed on this group. This includes links to other groups. Post s such as this will not be approved by Admins. • This group is intended to be a pleasant and helpful group where members can ask questions and receive help from other members and admins about freshwater aquatics. Any abusive or unpleasant comments towards other members or Admins will result in the comments being deleted and possibly the member removed from the group. We ask all members in the group to be vigilant and report any comments which they may feel are inappropriate as this will alert an Admin immediately to the comment. • Admin reserve the right to delete any comments giving advice that we feel is not in the best interests of the fish and to remove any member seen to repeatedly give poor or damaging advice. If you do offer advice, please make sure it is 100% correct. • The group does not condone the process of Fish-in Cycling, posts or comments encouraging and advising this may be removed and may result in the member being removed from the group. This does not mean members who may have been given bad advice and find themselves in a position where they must perform Fish-in Cycling cannot ask for help. This is of course allowed. • If it becomes necessary, the groups recommended procedure for Euthanasia for fish is the use of Clove oil, other comments referring to inhumane ways to do this will be removed and possibly result in the member being removed Any problems or concerns, please feel free to message group Admins/Moderators below: Admins: Sammie Chipperfield Paul Fryer David Morton Peter O'Callaghan Moderators: John Folkomer Laura Kimber Amanda Cerrato Morgan Phelps Crane

PLEASE share your information, petitions, pics or thoughts, here whenever and how often you want. But PLEASE post about elephants only. Feel free to add people that you think would enjoy this group and have the same love and respect for elephants and all animals as we do...the more the merrier. We are here for the elephants! Thanks!               <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Equestrians from "back in the day"
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 People who rode and showed horses back in the good old days -- 1990 and before. Please post stories and pictures across a variety of disciplines from BEFORE 1990. Younger equestrians invited as well to see how it used to be "back in the day." There is NO SELLING or ADVERTISING allowed in here. This rule also includes not using our member list for commercial (sales) purposes. Also when commenting please remember this group is not a 'critique my ride' group, its light hearted and fun. If you cannot make positive comments, please don't comment. Those who wish to log on to create drama will be removed. Also, it is also important to know that this group is in no way a "forum" to express negative or derogatory comments about people or photographs. Such comments will cause automatic removal. Where possible if posting downloaded photos it is helpful if the photographer can be credited and we require all photos to be identified completely. If a post's attachment is not able to be viewed by Members {"Attachment Unavailable"}, it is subject to deletion by the Admins. Should that occur, please feel free to repost so long as your privacy setting is changed to "Public" for that attachment, or you download what you want to share to your own computer or device and then upload it directly to this page. (Please also be sure to check where you got the original attachment, to see what the privacy settings are. If they aren't set for Public, we won't be able to see it if you just 'share' it.) Please also do not post anything as a share from private sites such as Pinterest or other websites which require a membership to see the photo. Your post will be deleted if you do so. Members of this page may not wish to become members of Pinterest or other pages in order to see photos. Also, we don't allow external Polls or Questions to be posted to this page, where the answers end up elsewhere. Should any member for any reason dislike a post or have an issue will they please, rather than get into a big dramatic argument on the thread, simply report the post to Admins. You can do that by going to the post, clicking on the down arrow to the upper right of it, and click on Report Post. Good wishes and enjoy being part of Equestrians from 'back in the day' Thank you for being part of this amazing group. --------Admin Team.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello, and welcome to So. Cal. Reptile Finder. Although this page has Socal as its name, we welcome any and all reptile posts from around the US! So make sure to post your products, and pictures with no bias whatsoever!!!! This page was created for people who love reptiles, love to share their thoughts, ideas, pics, and questions about them, and people who want to belong to a group where they will not be bashed or harrassed because of what they keep, what they like, and what they may be working with. I have selected a solid panel of admins who share a strong knowledge of reptiles,general husbandry, breeding,and a love for reptiles of all kinds!!!! If this sounds like something you'd like to be a part of, then by all means, come aboard!!!! Our admins are strongly committed to keeping out the troublemakers that you may have experienced on other forums, pages, chat rooms, and will make sure any people of that type are promptly dismissed!!! - Bryan

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Bird Meme’s. You are welcome to post funny pictures and videos of your birds, and other bird related posts. We just ask that you follow the rules of our group, or you will be banned. 1. No photos or videos of dead birds are allowed in the group. 2. No pictures, videos, posts, or comments regarding birds being with pets known as predators (i.e. cats, dogs, ferrets, etc...) 3. No blocking any moderators or admins. We can still see you, you are not hidden from anyone. So the only thing that will happen is you will be banned as soon as we see that you have blocked any of us. 4. No insulting, bullying, harassing, or otherwise impolite comments here, this is a friendly group that is made for everyone. Offending members will be banned from the group. 5. No politics, or religion will be tolerated in posts or comments. We respect all faiths, belief systems, ideologies, etc, but this is a place for bird posts and that is all. 6. Posts that are unrelated to birds and spam of any form will be deleted and the offending member will be banned from the group. 7. Recent duplicate posts are deleted. This is in the interest of keeping the page uncluttered and allowing everyone to keep seeing new content. 8. Posts are unavailable to us usually due to your own privacy settings, please check that before posting if this was checked after posting we cannot see it. Please check again and turn your settings on your post to public before re-submitting. 9. Posts must not endanger, or appear to endanger, the lives of birds in any way. 10. Any posts that appear to be discriminatory or offensive may be refused or removed at the moderators' discretion, and all mod/admin decisions are final. 11. No advertising parrot sales, craigslist posts, links to outside sources that sell/trade bird. 12. No advertising at all we have two sub groups for advertising. Bird Meme Artists, and Bird Meme Advertisements. 13. Do not spam links to your or any other group in comments or this will result in a ban (a helpful link is okay here and there just do not spam) 14. The Bird Memes Community is primarily an English speaking community, so we ask that all posts and comments be at least English friendly. 15. Posts from for profit organizations may not be accepted as they have been know to create false news for their benefit in the past. All posts will now have to be looked into more thoroughly. 16. While this is a group for posting Bird Memes, this is first and foremost a bird loving community, so all bird posts that follow the rules are allowed. Thanks! Enjoy all the birds &lt;3
                </div>
               </div>

                 Aging Horsewomen Intl. ™
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Aging Horsewomen Intl. Proudly featured in the #moretogether Facebook campaign. My goal in starting this group was a place for Aging Women to share their Horse Passion. Their Pictures. Their Joys and Triumphs. Their Concerns. Physical limitations and pain are frustrating and can be frightening when your love is a 1,200 pound flight animal. The realization one doesn’t bounce anymore is hard. It robs one of confidence. These concerns need shared to lighten the burden. Discussed for support and possible solutions. Aging (45 and above) Horsewomen want a drama free group. (We do allow younger women who for physical or emotional reasons identify with Aging.) Our first and most important Rule is Be Kind. In order to keep this site a pleasurable place for everyone, we ask that you take a couple of minutes of your time to read our Guidelines. When I have accepted your request to join I have invited you into my living room. Please read and follow my guidelines - Keep comments kind, positive, supportive - No political posts permitted. -No fundraising -No profanity. - No sales NO LINKS. - This group is not a format for your causes -Posts that include photos or videos of graphic injuries, must include a "Warning: Graphic photos/video in comments", on the original post so members can opt to scroll by if desired.- Posts that we encourage are those which are positive, uplifting, informational or humorous. Want to advertise to this group? Click here:https://aginghorsewomen.wordpress.com/ Once you have a Paid Ad on our website you may post once a week about your product or service on our Sister-Group Shopping with Aging Horsewomen. PLEASE READ THE ANNOUNCEMENTS. Complete Guidelines are there. It is your responsibility to read them when accepted into group.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Amanda To The Rescue (Fans)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Amanda Giese eased her troubled childhood by connecting with animals. They were her best friends, her "saving grace," she says. That connection continued into adulthood, leading her to start a nonprofit called Panda Paws Rescue, whose mission is to end homelessness, abuse and neglect of all animals. Alongside Amanda's kids, Jade and Beast, and partner Gary, the family cares for animals -- primarily dogs that others have given up on -- in need and helps them find loving forever homes. Those efforts are featured on hourlong episodes, including a large-scale rescue mission to save the lives of dozens of animals that have major medical or special needs.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Friends of Wolves
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 "For the strength of the Pack is the Wolf, and the strength of the Wolf is the Pack." Our goal is to save endangered wolves and to work towards creating a better future for them; one in which they are free to roam their natural habitat in peace and harmony. The more members we are, the more chances we have to be heard. Let us therefore speak up loud and clear, opposing the killing of wolves anywhere in the world for as long as we live. Let us all join our different forces and unite in support of the protection of all wolves around the globe. Let us stay determined to stand up against any injustice towards these magnificent creatures. Wolves MUST remain a protected species. Like all living creatures on earth, they deserve our full support and compassion, all being equally important and vital for a healthy Eco structure. Henry Beston said the following: "The animal shall not be measured by man. In a world older and more complete than ours, they move finished and complete, gifted with extensions of the senses we have lost or never attained, living by voices we shall never hear. They are not brethren; they are not underlings; they are other nations, caught with ourselves in the net of life and time, fellow prisoners of the splendor and travail of the earth." 
                </div>

                 Welcome to Herping the Globe... This group is a place to share some of your field herping adventures from around the world. "herpingtheglobe" PLEASE see the group rules before posting... EVERYONE PLEASE READ - GROUP RULES RULE 1 - Post MUST contain Scientific name of the animal and non specific location. RULE 2 - Posting is limited to 1 post per day (per member). RULE 3 - NO PETS... Images that look like the animal is a captive will be removed as well. RULE 4 - Photos that show careless handling, improper handling or if the animal appears to be stressed out... will be removed. RULE 5 - THIS IS NOT AN IDENTIFICATION GROUP... sorry. Ends up attracting all kinds of photos of dead snakes. This leads us back to the very first rule... anything without an ID is removed. RULE 6 - Be respectful... if you are out of line or just come to the group to be a pest, you will be exterminated. Feel free to post about a trip... include as many photos as you want in that post... Food, Lodging, Habitat, etc. Any animal posted should be clearly identified. This can be a great resource... whether you are posting about an eco tour you are leading or looking for information on a place you will be visiting or want to visit. That is why this group was created. If you have complaints... please direct them to our complaints department. Thanks all, Richard Cazares

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hummingbirds Anonymous is for those folks who can’t get through the day without at least looking at a photo of a Hummingbird. It’s for those whose heart, skips a beat, every time they see one of these fabulous flying jewels. If you’re one of those people, please join the group.. GUIDELINES FOR HUMMINGBIRDS ANONYMOUS MEMBERS  If you are requesting membership, please answer the questions when you ask to join.  This page is to primarily share photos and stories related to Hummingbirds. It provides a way for us to enjoy and learn more about these magical little birds.  No political comments, profanity, sarcasm or other questionable photos or statements allowed. If you see one of these, please “report to admin” button (top right arrow on the post), so it can be reviewed for appropriate action with possible member being removed from this forum.  Please add no more than 5 posts/or photos per day.  No debates on Red Dye allowed (no additives should be used). Please see our Album or under Announcements Section for safe recipes.  If you see a Hummingbird in distress, please see Announcements Section for Rehabbers near you. Note: We do not allow photos of dead birds of any kind.  Hand-made hummingbird items and crafts are allowed, although we take no responsibility for your purchase of any item you might see on this Forum.  If you have any questions or concerns, please PM us. These guidelines will be updated as necessary. (Your admin team: Deanna Frautschi, Mary L. Cessna, Kris Wilkerson, Michelle Crawford)

                 Cats Making Funny Faces
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Cats Making Funny Faces celebrates the most majestic of all beasts by sharing their not-so-majestic moments. The purpose of this group is to share pictures and other visual media (specifically cats making funny faces). Unlike other groups, we are strictly moderated and only allow funny/strange cat faces or poses on the weekdays. All other posts will be declined and ask that you resubmit on the weekend. Saturday and Sunday are free-for-all days where you can post anything cat-related RULES 1 - Cattos Making Funny Faces/Poses Only Mon - Friday : cats making funny faces/poses only Sat &amp; Sun : any cat-related content (as long as it abides by the other rules) Cats only. Other animals will be declined. 2 - No Sadposting no pet death posts - no animal abuse - no rehoming posts - no sad or sick looking strays/ferals - no adoption posts from rescues/shelters/fosters. This means text as well (no RIP, Rainbow Bridge, or details of past abuse) 3 - No Fighting or Name-Calling Absolutely no name-calling or bullying allowed. NO degrading comments or hate speech allowed. NO bigotry allowed! If you name call someone, you will probably get immediately booted. If someone starts a fight or calls you a name, please tag an admin 4 - No Negative Comments (be kind and courteous) Treat others the way you want to be treated. Ask yourself if what you're saying is necessary and/or kind. If you make neg. comments or accuse people of abuse in group, your comment will be deleted. (this includes negative comments about cats' weight - they are not wanted here) 5 - Do not comment on people's bodies or homes This should be obvious, but we have had a few issues. This is a cat group, not a judge people's appearances or home group.. 6 - No Blatant Advertising You may post your cat's instagram/twitter/facebook page with your pictures, but no products. 7 - Do Not Give Unsolicited Advice Don't give out unsolicited advice as it usually just comes off as critical and rude. We also may decline any post asking for advice as this is not an advice group. 8 - Troll Accounts Will Be Denied Membership If your account is obviously a troll account, we'll decline membership. Join on your real profile. You will also be declined if you have a bunch of offensive troll memes on your real profile. 9 - No Blocking Admins/Mods you will not be accepted to group or you will be removed if you're already in group. No exceptions. 10 - DMs &amp; PMs &amp; Friend Requests Do not message other members or send friend requests unless they've asked you to do so. Do not msg admins/mods why your post was declined or why you have to follow rules. Please do not post asking why your submission was declined. We simply don't have time to answer these messages in a group of 120K ppl. If we find out you are DMing or spam friend requesting many members, you WILL be removed.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Wild Bird, Wildlife, Nature Photography
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Wild Bird, Wildlife, Nature Photography (WBWNP). Post your own photographs of wildlife and natural landscapes. Posts that do not follow WBWNP guidelines are removed without notice. New members and those who have posts removed for cause may be temporarily placed on post approval. If your post does not appear or disappears, do not repost; reread these guidelines. If necessary, message an admin and include your photo. Members who repeatedly post images outside guidelines are blocked. * One photo per post. No videos. Up to 5 posts per day. * Do not post images showing people or any manmade objects! * Animals and plants depicted must be both wild and free. * Images must not be links. Confine links to post description. * Do not post images of nests with visible eggs or nestlings. * Set your post access to Public, so everyone can see it. * Every post must contain a photo you created. * No text on photo except copyright notice away from primary subject. * No copyrights or icons much larger or more distracting than average. * Do not post images resulting from live baiting. * No offers of goods or services on image or in post description. * No posts in support of causes or contests, no matter how worthy. * No digital art effects. No introduced elements not in the original scene. * No photos with primary subject out of focus or other serious defects. * No photos, large emojis, or other distracting elements in comments. * Do not add friends. Invite them to submit their own join requests. Manmade Objects: People, human hands, footprints, fences, buildings, roads, pathways, artificial surfaces, metal objects, signs, bridges, docks, dams, tents, cars, boats, planes, feeders, artificial perches, bird baths, nest boxes or platforms, power poles or lines, wire, cable, rope, cut stone, camera equipment, human-modified or arranged natural objects. Wild and Free: No pets. No cultivated plants or flowers or agricultural fields. No domestic, rescue, held, restrained, tethered, captive, caged, or zoo animals, or birds wearing jesses. Images of animals with tags, bands, and radio collars for the purpose of conservation research are permitted. WBWNP group goals and the rationale for every guideline: https://www.facebook.com/groups/WBWNP/permalink/2259349580989090 How to get more reactions to your posts: https://www.facebook.com/notes/wild-bird-wildlife-nature-photography/get-more-likes/2259349574322424/.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Real Cowboy 911
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Cowboy 911 is a worldwide group of people who pledge to offer assistance to others with livestock and pets in emergency situations. We offer a procedure manual and monetary assistance to facilitate the volunteers who rescue animals. Our members have specific skills, access, and equipment needed for livestock rescue. When disasters happen, thousands of small and large animals need evacuation and care. From pets to barnyard animals to wildlife. Assistance is needed when natural disasters strike. Ours is a voluntary movement, our members get involved in whatever capacity and skill they can offer. Volunteers are often the difference between life and death for the animals in need of evacuation. This is an immense service to the owners of these animals, many of whom feel their animals are family. In return the members of the group should be willing to do the same for each other, Because It's The Right Thing To Do! The Cowboy way. Helping another is its own reward. Let's get back to neighbors helping neighbors. After all, we are all friends and neighbors here!
                </div>

Sales / trades of aquatic plants are allowed. *Please be respectful to others, there may be a difference in opinions, but let's swallow our pride and act like adults. *Trading, selling, and buying of plants or tank equipment is encouraged, but please do not spam the group daily with them. *While religion and politics are a large part of our lives these days, please leave those discussions for other groups. *Pornography or trying to find a date here will get you banned permanently. *Group and Aquatic page shares allowed on Friday's and only if we can share on your page without having to ask permission. *No YouTube/Instagram plugs please. These will be deleted. *Planted Aquarium and Fish is in no way responsible for any trades, purchases, or sold items between members. Don't post problems here, resolve them among yourselves. *Please by all means don't be afraid to post an algae filled tank, or anything you might think is embarrassing as the help you gain through our members will benefit many others who are not as courageous as you.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Sulcata Tortoises
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Community Guidelines: 1) Always be respectful 2) No attacks on specific groups, profanity or any abusive language 3) No SPAM and Promoting groups for any reason 4) Please be careful dispensing personal information 5) No product placement (except for Sulcata products) 6) Take care of your tortoises! 7) Have fun! 8) Learn from each other 9) All deals, negotiations, requests, information exchanges, quips, videos, photos, comments, suggestions, advice and anything and everything pertaining to member-to-member contact remain independent and separate from the views and decisions of the administrative party of the group. 10) Admin staff are not liable for any and all unsolicited deals, arrangements and anything that lies within section nine (9), made between accounts of members non-members of the group. Anyone who infringes upon guidelines will be banned permanently from the group. We DO NOT tolerate any disrespectful/hateful comments, SPAM and the like. ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ Let's talk about our favorite turtles! Discuss times to meet up, show each other our pets, or perhaps seek advice on breeding and where to buy them. The African Spurred Tortoise (or the Sulcata) is native to Southern Africa. They are the third largest species of Tortoise in the world. When they breed, one female can lay several eggs. You will need to choose what kind of shelter to provide them with, and will need to make sure they are well fed, provided water and given appropriate care. Compared to other pets however, they are far less maintenance heavy. They are very fun to have and play with, and can eventually support massive weight on their back. They are our favorite pets. The best part is, they live. These tortoises can even live up to 80 years. The sulcata tortoise needs is currently threatened, and is at the vulnerable stage of its conservation status. We must work together to protect and care for these amazing creatures, to at least push them towards the less threatened category. 
                </div>
               </div>

                 Los Angeles Cats Kittens &amp; Kitties For Adoption
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! This is a support community for the page: https://www.facebook.com/LAAdoptCATS/ This group is for the community to share useful info and content related to cat life, cat ownership, cat lovers, and cat adoptions! To combat spam, scams, and unwanted clutter, all posts and posters must be approved first! NOTICE: IF YOU ARE ADOPTING OUT OR REHOMING CATS: FIRST post your ad(s) to our page: https://www.facebook.com/LAAdoptCATS/ Post your ad(s) to the community section on our page so that they can be verified and approved. Once approved, your ads will automatically disseminate across our network! ---------------------------------------- We love CATS and we're happy you're here. If you wish to be a member please follow these rules. Group Rules: #1 If you are posting a cat for adoption or rehoming: - You must have valid profile credentials to be approved. Details such as location (city/state), friends list, and some basic profile information should be visible so that viewers can evaluate your authenticity. - YOU MUST submit your ad(s) to our Facebook Page: https://www.facebook.com/LAAdoptCATS/community to be vetted and approved. (Once approved, your ad(s) will disseminate across our network.) #2 Cat Post Guidelines: If you are posting a cat for adoption or rehoming, please include the following: - Clear, tasteful pictures of the pet (no text on the pictures, phone numbers or contact info) - Location, gender, age, breed and pertinent background info - Adoption or rehoming information and costs - Contact Information #3 If you are a member of this group: - No Negative/Hate Speech or Bullying. Be friendly and courteous. #4 If you are posting in this group: - Do not submit posts IN SEARCH OF... a cat or any particular feature (breed, gender, age...etc)... browse our pages and website instead! - Please keep posts related to cat life, cat ownership, cat lovers, and cat adoptions! Posts about lost CATS are allowed! - No Promotions or Spam. Self promotion or irrelevant links are not allowed. Keep posts content driven. - All posts must be approved first - only useful information that is helpful to the community will be permitted! #5 If you are adopting pets: - Make sure to exercise due diligence and investigate the person you’re dealing with - Report kitten mills, illegal, or inhumane behavior - Don’t electronically send money to people you do not know or have not met. Deal with people in person for safety. - No one is responsible for your safety or actions but you. This is an organic and natural community and you alone are responsible for protecting yourself and ensuring you don’t get scammed. Exercise due diligence with everyone you deal with. #6 We are in this together, to create a welcoming environment. Give more to the group than you take. Be Kind and Courteous. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. If you see violations to the rules please report them to the moderators.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">

This is a place to post photographs and videos depicting WILD OWLS exhibiting natural behaviour within their natural habitat. Any owl-related questions including ID queries are also welcome. Please note that the elected format of this group is POST APPROVAL therefore all posts will be screened by an administrator or moderator. Please read and follow the rules upon admittance to this group. We look forward to your contributions and participation!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Snakes for Beginners &amp; Beyond
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Current Group Rules: 1. Keep swearing and vulgarity to a minimum, let’s keep it classy! 2. Constructive criticism is great. There’s always a way to express concern or offer advice respectfully. If anyone is here to belittle, bash, bicker, or troll, they will be removed promptly. 3. Share anything Snake related 🙂 4. Live feeding videos are not allowed. Should you have any questions in regards to feeding live, feel free to ask or send a PM to an admin or mod. 5. If a practice is deemed unsafe or inhumane (feeders), the comment, post or picture will be removed &amp; poster may be muted or removed from the group. 6. Please, no pictures or posts about cohabbing. If you would like to learn about cohabbing, please see the file in the “Files” section of the group. This is a very touchy subject for many keepers. 7. Please no sharing of any screenshots of the group, or using other peoples’ pictures without permission. 8. Please limit negative talking of other groups on Facebook. We don’t want to engage in that type of thing here, our goal is SB&amp;B (Snakes for Beginners &amp; Beyond) and I would like to keep our focus on our members ☺️ 9. Sales are not allowed 03/22/19. Sharing business pages, posts from them or other social medias are only allowed ON THE SOCIAL SUNDAY POST, which is posted on... Sundays by an admin ⭐️ 10. There will be no free/rehoming snakes or go fund me/charity/raffle posts allowed without admin approval. Note: While Native/Wild Snake ID requests are not prohibited, we suggest asking at the group called Snake Identification should be prioritized. This is a group mainly for the care of captive snakes- and does not promise any perfect IDs of wild snakes. Please refrain for “guessing”. The following Days will have Themes: Sunday: Social Sunday! Comment your sales or your social media pages in the Share Sunday Posting! Monday: Show Me Mondays! Comment a pic of your snake for the chosen topic! Most liked pics get into the hall of fame album 🤩 Tuesday: Trivia Tuesday! Wednesday: Whatever Wednesday! Share pictures of your other pets - or whatever! On Wednesdays! Thursday: Theme Thursdays! We’ll ask to share a picture or story of a given theme! A picture will then be chosen as a group banner! Friday: Feature Friday 😃 We will discuss a featured topic for the week ! Saturday: Safety Saturday! A topic will be discussed in regards to safety 🙂 Feel free to ask any questions! Admin Team: Denee Marie Jordan Nicole Trahin Lex Martinez Jason Farrow Andrea Boa Jessica Jean Christian Alek Ally Martinez

                 ADMINS: Keira Mastro-Battista, Erin Cox, Gabriel Aloisio, Kaitlyn Nicole Wright, Olivia Campbell MODERATORS: Jestie Kelly, Becca Cleveland tag us if something needs dealing with RULES: 1. DON'T BE AN ASSHOLE / BE KIND AND COURTEOUS Respect your group members, admins and mods. Add CW/TW's if needed/asked. Trolling will earn a mute, followed by a ban. We don't have to justify said decisions if your behaviour speaks for itself. 2. NO BULLYING, DEROGATORY SPEECH, ETC. Outright malicious behaviour with the intent to make someone's day miserable will be an instant ban, no exceptions. This includes, but is not limited to: bullying, slurs, prejudice, hate speech etc. 3. RESPECT EVERYONE'S PRIVACY Don't go public. Don't message members without permission. Don't profile stalk. Doxxing will lead to an instant ban, followed by a deletion of the original post. 4. NO INTENTIONALLY INFLAMMATORY BEHAVIOUR Avoid posting controversial or irrelevant content for the sake of provoking or inciting argumentative, aggressive or abusive behaviour and responses. This is a group for cats misbehaving, not humans. 5. NO POSTING DEAD OR MAIMED ANIMALS This includes cats holding critters in their mouths. We all know cats like to hunt, it's not norty, it's natural. Not everyone likes seeing dead/suffering animals. These posts will be deleted 6. NO UNSOLICITED ADVICE Please don’t post advice unless a thread is specifically asking for it. This includes medical advice. Posting unsolicited advice will lead to a mute and then a ban. the password is toebeans 7. ADD CW/TWS WHEN NECESSARY OR ASKED Anything with particularly sensitive content will need a content warning. Any images with distressing content will need to be nested properly, and they will be removed if they are in the main post. 8. TAG A MOD/ADMIN If a comment or post needs our attention in any way, do not use the report function (it could get our group zucced). Please tag one of the team. We're here to help. Admin decisions are final.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 *MISSING PETS ACROSS AMERICA "BRING THEM HOME" Please post: City, State &amp; Phone (contact so important, get a pay as you go if concern over privacy) So many dangers. People are busy, help them help your beloved family member to safety. *Goal is to Help Get The Word Out Far &amp; Wide to Increase Chances to Get Pets Home Safe: Group is open to everyone. Anyone trying to help find a pet or pet owner can post here. Quicker the word gets out the better chances to find your pet. *Photos are a good thing to do at least one time on all pages and groups. They are quickest and easiest ways for people to cross ref when a pet is found. Links can take hours to get to a month later where picture posts take minutes to view. Include: A.) City, State &amp; Phone B.) Pets Description: color, size, etc. C.) Date Last Seen or found D.) Contact Information – email, phone or website with information Please Post Anything to Help Find Missing Pets at: http://www.facebook.com/missingpetsusa ********************************************** Our Only Goal is to get Pets to Safety. It does not matter how it happened or who is at fault. The only thing matters, is getting the Pets Information Out in an Alert. They Could Be In Danger! Thru the pain of losing a pet, realized there is much help needed for pets that are lost or stolen. Please realize stolen pets are usually dumped or sold quickly. Chances are who has them has no idea they have a loving owner. For the safety of your pet it is always best to say Lost or Missing. Many places let us list our missing, lost &amp; found pets. Yet way to many are never recovered. Believe this Group of Friends Support we can get a pets info out Far &amp; Wide. Greatly increasing chances of getting our pets home safe &amp; quickly. Wish to use this Group like an Amber Alert for Missing Pets. "Dog / Pet Theft is not an epidemic but it is Tragic to Families." It has happened to too many families already. The Internet is a great source of information we need to utilize it. All Missing Pets Can Be Posted for Everyone - Anywhere. Thankful for everyone here &amp; how they ban together for the animals! Wish to possibly prevent cases like Smiley's from happening to others. Having an Emergency Plan in Place is a Step in the Right Direction. Hope every animal lover &amp; pet owner joins to help them Home Safe Global HELP for LOST &amp; FOUND PET's. http://www.facebook.com/note.php?note_id=146276862049632&amp;id=133710206661162 FINDING MISSING, STOLEN, LOST PETS or FOUND Pets Owner. http://www.facebook.com/note.php?note_id=146276862049632 Helpful step by step also if pet is stolen. http://www.doggiemanners.com/art_finding_stolen_dogs.html Our Dog was never found but he helped save many others. Thank you all so much for your support. Smiley's human mom "Never Give Up"

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Jockey World is a 501(c)(3) non-profit educational organization in horse racing created by former award-winning jockey Frankie Lovato Jr. Dedicated to providing reliable information, tools, guidance and resources, that includes knowledge in health &amp; safety, to anyone who wishes to pursue a career or develop a better understanding of the horse racing industry. Jockey World is not a gambling related organization. IMPORTANT MESSAGE TO ALL JOCKEY WORLD MEMBERS: It has always been strict policy that posts selling products and/or advertising products and services are not allowed unless you are a sponsor of Jockey World. Please contact us at info@jockeyworld.org for more info if you would like to become a sponsor. Also any political, religious or slaughter issues should not be discussed here in Jockey World. We must not draw away from our mission with Jockey World and all of our members. Such content with politics, religion &amp; slaughter can cause and divide even the best friendships. Such content is best promoted and discussed in the appropriate platforms where awareness, support and efforts can best suit and rally for those who diligently work so hard on this issue. Jockey World is not that platform. We do approve and support any affiliate charities and fundraising efforts towards all horse rescues, thoroughbred retirement foundations and other similar programs that allow us all to embrace "in harmony" our love for horses. Please contact us at info@jockeyworld.org for approval prior to posting. Thank you for understanding.

                 The Bird Identification Group of the World
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Facebook ID group of the world. As the name implies, this group is specifically for the concise, detailed discussion of bird ID issues of bird species from around the world, advanced discussions about field ID and related issues, the concise and detailed discussion of ID of unknown birds (photos included and encouraged) and for the purpose of providing ID tips on birds from around the world for those who want to learn and don't mind scrounging through various discussions. The group is intended to be welcoming and inviting not just to advanced birders, but to everyone from beginner on up who wish to learn more about bird ID. Please keep this in mind when posting/commenting. Note: IF YOU DO NOT FOLLOW THE RULES, AND ESPECIALLY, IF YOU SIMPLY POST PHOTOS TO SPAM THE GROUP OR TRY TO SELL ANYTHING, YOU WILL BE BANNED. PERIOD. Any photo or text post that is posted that is not requesting an ID, can be considered spam. IF YOU HAVE NOT READ THE RULES, PLEASE DO NOT POST TO THE GROUP! THE LINK IS BELOW. CLICK ON IT! Before posting/commenting in the group, please read the group Rules/Guidelines that are in the pinned post at the top of the discussion page. FYI: the admin cannot be here to moderate 24/7, so please help out by reporting posts that infringe upon these rules.

Any further violations of this rule will result in removal and blocking. #6. Please stick to the mission statement of this group. Members are encouraged to report any post or comment they feel violates the rules of this group or Facebook. If you aren't sure, feel free to message the Admin or Mod. Our objective is to provide you the best information about owning and taking care of an Iguana as a pet. We do this through this blog and a community of like minded people

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 911 Parrot Alert (Official)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to 911 Parrot Alert an international and volunteer based group dedicated to reuniting lost and found birds. Our goal is to equip our members with the necessary tools and knowledge needed in order to reunite lost and found birds back with their families. 911 Parrot Alert has outlined some pertinent steps that should be taken in the event you have lost or found a bird which can be found directly In our PINNED POST located at the very top of the group page. Please read our group rules in full if you have not yet done so. You are expected to follow these rules, and failure to do so may result in being removed without warning. *** 911 PARROT ALERT'S HOUSE RULES *** 1. Please be respectful of all members, admin and moderators. 2. Any disrespectful, critical and unhelpful comments will be deleted. Do not suggest wing clipping at any time. 3. Please keep all posts on topic and in relation to lost, found or stolen birds. 4. Do not post or ask for leg band/ring numbers. This information should remain private as this is an owner's proof of ownership. 5. Do not post photos of deceased birds. 6. Do NOT suggest, imply or ask finders for found birds nor make comments such as “I’ll take it”or "I can foster", etc. Do NOT send private messages to finders seeking to adopt a found bird. If you are a finder and have been contacted by someone in this group wanting a bird you found, please forward a copy of the screenshot along with their name to one of our Admins or Moderators so we can handle it accordingly. We believe pets are family and our goal on 911 Parrot Alert is to reunite ALL BIRDS back with their families. 7. Any and all GoFundMe/crowdfunding campaigns,buy/sell, spam or off topic posts will be removed. 8. Do Not Block Admin or Moderators. 9. 911 Parrot Alert DOES NOT recommend the use of firetrucks, tree services, large equipment, water hoses, lifts, ladders, towels, nets, etc. in order to retrieve a bird. (Except in extreme circumstances of imminent physical danger to the bird) Please refrain from making these type of suggestions to our members as these comments will be deleted. 10. Please familiarize yourself with 911 Parrot Alert's Search &amp; Retrieve Protocol. https://drive.google.com/file/d/0B78YYzbJx75hMmZyM3J1S3ZiLTg/view?usp=sharing GUIDELINES WHEN POSTING TO 911 PARROT ALERT 1. When posting to 911 Parrot Alert please include species of parrot lost or found, date lost or found, city, state and contact information. 2. When sharing a post to 911 Parrot Alert, please double check to see if that post has already been shared to 911 Parrot Alert as duplicate posts are removed. 3. How to search 911 Parrot Alert's group page for posts. Please go to the search bar located in the column on the left hand side of the group page 'Search this group' and type in species &amp; state or city &amp; state into the search bar to bring up any posts in connection with your search. (ie Cockatiel FL or Miami FL). Thank you, 911 Parrot Alert
                </div>
