                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Hummingbird Migration Sighting
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Description New Members please read description before first post. If your heart skips a beat every time you see one. or hear the gentle whirl noise and turn to see where she's off too If you're one of those people, you are in the best place possible Guidelines : This is a page to share photos and stories about your hummingbirds. It also allows us to post important information during spring and fall migration NO SELLING ! Due to the growth of the group and to assure everyone that the people joining really want to be here, we are temporarily suspending members inviting friends. If your friends show a real interest, give them the group link and let them join on their own please rather than 50 or more people at a time leaving after you joined then .without their permission... Be Kind We're all in this together to create a welcoming environment. Let's treat everyone with respect. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. Please give more than you take to this Facebook page. Self-promotion, spam and irrelevant posts aren't allowed. This group is about hummingbirds, their care, feeding and of course photos Photos: Please only post your own photos, no one else's. No photos of praying mantises harming hummingbirds and.or injured or dead hummingbirds. We have seen the photos repeatedly and we find photos not necessary to make the point.If you post a photo, you will be removed.. no questions asked How to Keep Ants Out of Your Hummingbird Feeder Attention: Please do not add Vaseline or oil of any kind to bird feeder poles .anywhere a bird could come in contact with a oil. This will be life threatening. You can either get a hummingbird feeder with a built-in ant moat, attach a guard or moat to your existing feeder or make your own. If you do not have a hummingbird feeder with an ant moat already built-in then you can add one by attaching it between the feeder and the hanger rod You simply fill the moat with water and ants go in, but they can't get out - and more importantly, they can't get to your hummingbird feeder. Red Dye is not necessary to attract hummingbirds. The feeders made today along with flowers or other colourful displays in your backyard are sufficient.. Neither is food coloring of any kind, they are not required to attract the hummingbirds and are not advised. Facebook Admin : Darlin Bonchek Caryl Clemens Lynn Newell Gary Wehrie

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello everyone and welcome to Kitten Happiness! This is a cat lovers group. We hope that you will find this to be your happy and fun loving place here where you can discuss about everything regarding cats. Please read the rules and join us - have fun!! If you see a post that shouldn't be here, please report the post and NOT the group. Reporting the group gets admin accounts locked out and can result in limited use of Facebook, with certain features such as messaging and admin abilities not working. Also, reporting the group can shut the entire group down and myself and the other admins would be VERY upset if that were to happen. You can message us and one of admins will look into the situation as soon as possible. RULES OF THE GROUP: 1. You must be 13 to be on Facebook, so there should not be anyone younger than that in here. 2. Respect all the fellow members of the group and the admins please. We will ban anyone that is nasty or rude. If you don't like something that's posted, you can hide it from your view or just scroll on by. If you think i needs to be removed, report it to an admin or message one of us.Please respect your fellow member's post and opinions. Also, respect the admins. If they remove your post or comment, it is for good reason. If you have any complaints, please message them directly. 3. No Foul Language PLEASE. Use of bad language will result in immediate ban. Political posts will result in a permanent ban. Hence no political posts. No Debates/Arguments. 4. Absolutely NO fundraisers are permitted! If you post one, it will be removed and you will be banned. 5. This isn't a business page and hence no selling on this group. No sale posts, even if they are cat or cat item related. You're welcome to show off your work and link to your business page but no listing items for sale or asking other members if they are interested in purchasing what you're selling. If you are interested in someone's work, please send them a private message or inquire on their business page. 6. NO STEALING OF PHOTOS. Please do not post a photo you got from the internet and claim it as your own. Likewise, if you want to share a post from the group, please ASK PERMISSION FIRST from the owner before sharing. 7. No gruesome pictures or stories of animal abuse please. 8. Please help us keep the group atmosphere clean. We will then make a happy family with our cute kittens. 9.Any images or videos shared in the group can be used by us to post to other community pages. You are giving us the rights to use the file without restrictions. You confirm that you have full copyright and publishing rights to the uploaded file and associated information. We may alter the uploaded file by adding text, watermarks or other changes we choose to make. You understand that we may post your file at any time in the future at our own discretion without notice. 10. Do not add linked posts from a blog. Thank you guys!! Admins: David Hirschfeld Prachi Joglekar

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Cheetahs Only
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Not only is the Cheetah the fastest land animal in the world today, the species has been in existence for between 3.5 and four million years - making it the oldest of Earth’s big cats. Slender bodies, long legs and a flexible spine help the Cheetah achieve speeds in excess of 100kph in pursuit of its prey, with its tail acting as a finely-tuned balancing aid. It also has semi-retractable claws and cannot roar like other big cats. Habitat Native to savannahs or grasslands in eastern and southern Africa and some parts of Iran, the species was once found across Asia and Europe. Wild Notes The Cheetah has a carnivorous diet - feeding on smaller animals including hares, young antelope and birds - but while it is skilled at stalking and killing prey, it tends to lose up to half of its kill to larger predators. Females are solitary creatures - in contrast to males, who live in groups - and give birth to between three and six cubs that have a thick mane of grey fur down their back. Cubs are thought to mimic the ferocious African Honey Badger initially as the animal is not particularly good at defending either itself or its young and will sprint away from danger rather than risk being injured. The mother will leave the cub group at 18 months, with any females venturing out of their own after two years. Conservation The high mortality rate of cubs in the wild (up to 90%) is a key reason why the species is now listed as Vulnerable, with the situation in Asia now considered to be Critical. Breeding programmes have been established to try and reverse this trend but other threats include disease, habitat loss and conflict with man if near livestock areas. Did you know? Despite the Cheetah’s ability to reach high speeds, it can only maintain the effort for about 60 seconds. Any increase in body temperature - even by a couple of degrees - can actually lead to irrecoverable brain damage. Cheetahs often need to rest for up to half an hour to allow their blood cool after a chase. 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 English Tack Exchange
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 PLEASE READ!! This group is intended as a buying and selling group for ENGLISH TACK and ENGLISH RIDING APPAREL ONLY! Items such as (but not limited to) Jewelry and Decals are NOT tack. Please use the "Sell Something" option tab when posting. We have a zero tolerance policy- so break a rule, we have the right to block and ban permanently with or without warning (our discretion) so READ THESE!! EVERY post and picture MUST contain the following in the description area, not the comments and not under the picture. 1. ALL posts with an item for sale must be done through the sell tab at the top of page with a price, description and pictures on the main post. If you do not have these three requirements your post will be deleted with no notice. If you are ISO of something please use the discuss tab. Please do not list a generic "I have lots of stuff for sale, let me know what you're looking for..." post. If you say "Make an offer" or "what's this worth" we'll assume $5 is acceptable, including shipping. - Description- size, condition, color, defects - Picture (of your actual item). If there is damage to the item, please disclose this upfront in the original post and before accepting payment. - Price for each respective item- we don't allow make a offer etc. All pricing MUST BE LISTED and in $USD. 4. If you have bumped an item 3 times with no interest, consider lowering your price or removing your item. 5. “Holding” an item is technically up to the seller’s discretion, but is discouraged. The item is not “sold” until it is paid for in full. As such, we recommend that sellers use a “first to pay for it, gets it” mentality. While not best practice, the seller has the option of changing their price until the item has been paid for. 6. No Hijacking: Do not try to buy or sell your item on someone else's post. If you have the same item make your own for sale post. If someone else is looking for something or did an ISO post, do not comment saying you are looking for the same item. 7. We do not allow outside links to groups, businesses, websites, non profits, page promotions or other forms of advertising. ie: photography, hair bows, jewelry, toys, etc. 8. We advise against other forms of payment aside from PayPal. Trades, money orders, and other forms of payment are less secure and as such, do not provide protection for either party. BUYERS BEWARE- if you feel like something is off- do not buy the item. 9. If you are having an issue with a group member or suspect fraud/scam, please contact an admin directly. Do not post it on the site for everyone to see. We try to keep our site as friendly and drama free as possible. We will help as much as we can, assuming that the parties are members of the group and that the individual transaction originated here. 10. IF YOU BLOCK AN ADMIN OR DISAGREE W/ WHAT WE HAVE STATED, YOU WILL BE BANNED. 11. Use common sense and be respectful of others and of the admin’s decisions.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Awesome Elephants!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for those of us who love the amazing elephant - nature's gentle giant! Please, post ONLY ELEPHANT-RELATED materials. Pictures, videos, artworks, cartoons, collections, petitions, etc. This GROUP HAS 2 RULES: RESPECT OTHER MEMBERS and DO NOT USE FOUL LANGUAGE! Inappropriate posts will be deleted! Before you post a picture - THINK! Ask yourself - is this a behaviour that an elephant in its natural habitat would exhibit? If the answer is "no", then it is likely an elephant that has been abused in order to do something unnatural like paint or walk on its hind legs. Before you post a picture of a baby, ask yourself where its mother is and where the herd is. If you are unsure whether a picture you wish to post is an abuse to an elephant, please feel free to inbox me before posting. This group does not support poaching, hunting, circuses, or elephants being used for any form of entertainment, including temple elephants, babies being used to make money on the beach, elephants painting, or elephant back rides/treks. We are all part of this group for the same reason - to love and admire natures most magnificent creature and to bring awareness to the plight of the elephant. Please respect the groups rules and also, please respect each other. People learn far more with kindness and patience than with anger and personal attacks. Advertising will only be allowed if it is elephant-related or supports elephants. Say NO to ivory!! Say NO to any abuse of elephants!
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Funny Cats
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Watching funny cat videos has become a national pastime. Ask anyone if they have ever indulged in a funny cat video or two and chances are you will get an answer in the affirmative. In fact, there are even gatherings of thousands of people at yearly internet cat video festivals. Why this funny-cat-video phenomena? There are recent studies that prove that watching funny cat videos is actually really good for you, in addition to just being a crazy amount of fun. Research shows that binge-watching some really funny cat videos results in a reduction of stress, a boost in energy levels, and an increase in feelings of happiness and well-being. The results are so impressive that they are even considering using funny cat videos as therapy, to which I reply, “Yes, please!” I think this is all the excuse that I and my fellow funny-cat-video lovers need to sit back, relax, and indulge in a collection of the most hilarious viral cat videos.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Dogspotting
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 What is Dogspotting? 1. A sport and lifestyle of spotting random dogs. 2. Classifying the nature of the spot according to the rule set. 3. Assigning a score or sharing the spot for peer scoring. 4. A fun place to hang out with friends and enjoy dogs. PLEASE read the Pinned Thread for ALL of the rules before posting in the group! Complete Lists of Current Group Info &amp; Rules: https://www.facebook.com/groups/dogspotting/permalink/10157857040014467/ Rule Slides: (Fun, hisorical, classic Dogspotting Info; please use the link above for a current list of Rules and info- the link below shows past rules and other interesting info) https://www.facebook.com/DogspottingRules/posts/955966677836871 #1 Rule, don’t post yer own dog or a dog that you know! If it's your own dog, a dog you have met before, or a dog you know exists, it is ineligible for submission as a spot! Visit our sister group, Dogspotting Society, where you CAN post your own dog and also many other types of things that are ineligible in this group: https://www.facebook.com/groups/DogspottingSociety/ 🐾🐾🐾OTHER IMPORTANT LINKS 🐾🐾🐾 Dogspotting Peoples Court (Contact here to contest bans under the court of law) https://www.facebook.com/DogspottingCourt/ Dogspotting Media: https://www.facebook.com/dogspottingmedia/ Dogspotting Shop: https://dogspotting.teemill.com/Dogspotting Dogspotting Instagram: https://instagram.com/dogspottingorg/ Dogspotting Snapchat: @DogspottingOrg Dogspotting Twitter: https://twitter.com/dogspottingorg HQ Website: http://www.dogspotting.dog/ DS TRIUMVIRATE Jeff Wallen - Director of Dog Organization - President Dogspotting LLC Molly Bloomfield - Director of Moderator and Member Operations Ruth Esther Wollman - Director of Human-Dog Relations - Pro Bone-o Legal Aid Jason L'Eane - Director of Dog Fungi Yamber Brzez - Bork Keeper - Social Media Manager DS SENATE (COMMITTEE OF PUBLIC SAFETY): Ally Saltford Benjamin Royer Brooke Bates Callie May Carl Jenkins Carolann Fiore Carolyn Steinberg Cassie Close Catherine Leem Debbie Nanni Fan Pan Hannah Hans Hunter Workman Jarrod McLean Jillian Holt Maika Greer Maura Smith Max Sovngarde Megan Lesko Michelle Dewing Oscar Jacob Raphael Fischer Saran Morgan Sergio Opmaco Stephen Treloar Størmy Kyne Tiberius Bertea Tobias Brockie Tricia Smith DS Advisors: John Savoia - Dog Guru and Visionary (current whereabouts unknown) Reid Paskiewicz - Director of Dog Operations - VP Dogspotting LLC Marty Kimmel - DogTech Director - Dogspotting CTO David Thorpe -Official Dogspotting Historian -Record Keeper, and Pro Gamer Josh Boruff -Bad man -Creator of the Orthodox scoring system ✴We are NOT a cult ✴ ✴The Dogs are the Life ✴ ✴The Dogs Must Flow ✴ Dogspotting® is a Trademarked Entity.

                 Dolphin Way Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group for discussions on the subject of dolphins, their close relatives and the issues affecting them. The policy in this group is that it is about dolphins. So please stay roughly on topic or your posts may be removed. For example, although there are some wonderful causes and campaigns that are very worthy that you may want to promote; but if they are not related to dolphins, please do it somewhere more appropriate. You can recommend anyone to join and they will normally be automatically accepted (or they can apply themselves) but the group is moderated by administrators to keep out disruptive people or spammers. The site is also a place where you can discuss the novel, Dolphin Way: Rise of the Guardians by Mark Caney. We are very happy for you do that, but remember not everyone has read it yet — so don’t give away the ending! See www.facebook.com/DolphinWay and www.dolphin-way.com for more details. If you want to get the book search in your favourite online store or local bookshop and use this ISBN number: 978-1-90549-223-7 (or in some systems this one: 1905492235). You can also get it as an e-book.

                 Adopt A Living Legend
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This page is for anyone to post BLM or Forest Service Mustang on that are needing rehomed, Available for adoption or for sale. Please, no domestic bred horses. Please post HMA, age, where the horse is located, and adoption/price. POST ONLY horses you personally own/foster, or have PERMISSION from owner to post This can be a valuable resource for helping get mustangs adopted. No politics, No controversy please. As a co-moderator of this group, I would like to request if SAFER or any other rescue or sanctuary or private party has BLM horses they are offering up for sale or adoption, STATE IN YOUR ORIGINAL POST the restrictions, such as not leaving the state the rescue is in for a year, or not receiving ownership of the horse, etc. Thank you! Also, if you are trying to join and have not been approved, it is most likely because you have no current friends in this group. We check the walls of all those who request to join and if there is no indication of equine activity, membership will be DENIED. If you are not a scammer and have not been approved, please message me and explain how being a member of this group is beneficial to you and the members. Thank you!

               <div class="_8wo2"></div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Leopard Gecko Care and Advice
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  Leopard Gecko Care and Advice is a family friendly group, geared towards basic beginner care. We are a care and advice group and will give advice when needed. We have tons of information and resources in our files, and many knowledgeable members willing to assist you with information on your new pet. PLEASE READ THE FILES WE HAVE PROVIDED AND USE THE SEARCH FUNCTION BEFORE MAKING NEW POSTS: chances are, your question has been asked before. The Group Rules! 1. Be respectful. Being direct is allowed, being rude is not. Flex your tactful muscles! Imagine how you would like things explained to YOU. 2. No foul language. A list of banned words can be found in the files section. 3. Do not make a post complaining about the group or to tell us you are leaving. Please direct issues regarding the group to the admins via PM. Regarding problems with a post/thread, please use the “report to admin” feature. 4. Pet store bashing posts are not allowed. Take your complaints to the appropriate corporate leader. Contact info can be found in the files. 5. Posts/comments are not to be deleted unless done by an admin. Do not turn off commenting on your post either. Use the “turn off notifications” feature if you no longer want to be a part of a thread. 6. We like to keep all questions in the group and prefer no PM'ing between members. We are not responsible for misinformation given in private messages. If another member is sending you unwanted, rude, or threatening messages, please send screen shots to an admin right away. 7. GoFundMe and other donation based posts prohibited unless approved by the admin team. 8. Promoting unsafe practices, including but not limited to: loose substrate, cohabitation, and home remedies for injuries or illness are strictly prohibited and may result in a ban. “I have done so for X amount of time and never had a problem” IS considered promoting. 9. If an admin asks you to stop doing something, there's a reason for it. Do not continue. If an admin asks you a question, please answer it. There are reasons for asking what we do to help you. 10. Blocking admins will result in removal from the group. Blatant disregard of rules, admin instructions, or corrections to misstated facts are also subject to no-warning removal from group. 11. Limit all Craigslist or any other type of sales/rescue posts to the classified or rescue groups only. 12. Use the search bar at the top chances are it's been answered many times before. Rules subject to change and individual interpretation *at admin discretion*. For a list of Admins and Moderators; https://www.facebook.com/groups/LeopardGeckoCareAdvice/admins/?ref=group_cover This is the caresheet we have found to be the most up to date and have the safest care practices that we promote in this group. Please have a read through. http://lizardbeans.tumblr.com/post/109818693654/leopard-gecko-care
                </div>

                 Birds went extinct in the 50's and the government replaced them with spy drones that look like birds. Get with the program or get out. All discussion should revolve around the fact that birds aren't real. Rules: 1. Please keep all posts relevant to the fact that so called "birds" are actually government surveillance drones. We encourage lively debate about the nature, purpose, and uses of these drones. We also welcome the "bird-curious" in our group, but please do not post any pro-bird propaganda. 2. On the topic of pro-bird propaganda, we do not allow posts that try to prove the existence of "birds" by showing doctored pictures of "birds" having flesh or entrails. We also do not allow pictures of dead animals. 3. Finally, please keep discussion civil and centered around birds not being real. We are not here to debate any political beliefs or ideologies. We hope that people of varying backgrounds can work together to uncover this government conspiracy without allowing unrelated differences to get in the way.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 IGUANA LOVERS
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hey everybody and welcome to IGUANA LOVERS! We are here to help give answers to all of your iguana questions, give solutions to problems, and to just have some fun and share our beautiful creatures and their amazing habitats we have built or purchased for them. *** Rules*** 1. NO ANIMAL SALES OR REHOMING POSTS. 2. NO Swearing, cursing ...Facebook has keyword alerts in place. we will get the notification and remove the comment. No name calling, rude, abusive drama .... This is a public page and there are many young ones about...Keep it clean, respectful and polite. 3. No posts of dead animals. This includes hunted iguanas or for food. Educational posts medical surgeries and iguanas that have passed are acceptable with appropriate warnings / captions. 4. No spamming, it will be deleted 5. No blocking admins. You will be removed from the group. 6. No bashing any big corporate pet stores. 7. Blatant cursing "F" bombing and other vulgarity will not be tolerated. You will be asked to edit or remove the offenses in order to keep the group appropriate for all ages. 8. NO TROLL POSTS....we will delete it. 9. Please keep posts relegated to iguana species. Yes we love many creatures, but this is an iguana forum. You may see your post deleted if it strays too far off. 10. We do NOT condone or allow members to recommend the feeding of animal based protein to green iguanas. 11. No stealing or sharing photos of members without their permission and claiming it as yours. 12. No "Go fund me posts". 13. Don't offer questionable advice or jump into disagreements just because you want to be visible. 14. No soliciting to join other groups OR FOLLOW you ...your post will be deleted. We are not your launch pad to get your group started and that includes YOUTUBE and INSTAGRAM Breaking any of these rules will potentially cost you the privilege of being part of this group. Any questions, problems, or concerns, please don't hesitate to message an admin. Mondays are known as #mpm (My Pets Monday) where posts of your other pets are allowed in the group. Thanks! -Admins 🐉

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Husky Addicts
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Husky Addicts! Below are some rules but we still want this page to be as fun as possible for everybody! 1. Have fun! But be courteous! You must be respectful at all times. Rudeness will not be tolerated or you will be removed and blocked from the group. 2. No promoting of other pages...personal or business...No selling of any products. 3. Talk about wolf dogs is allowed. But please proceed with caution. If you post your picture of your "wolf dog" without proper DNA testing, you will be muted. We do NOT allow misrepresentation. 4. We do not allow the misrepresentation of service dogs. If you are advertising your dog as a service dog, and we find evidence that it is not, your post will be deleted. We would like to keep actual service dogs in this group safe, as well as protect owners from the repercussions of claiming a fake service dog. 5. As we have members from all around, sales, fostering and rehoming posts are not allowed. Please use your local Facebook groups for this. 6. While health/medical advice posts are allowed, please remember we are not the expert and we always recommend a vet's opinion! 7. Training tools: these are simply tools. No berating or talking down to someone who uses training tools. For example, shock collars, prong collars, muzzles, choke collars etc. An admin will simply delete your comments without warning. If it continues, this will result in banning you. 8. No blocking admins. Doing so will results in one warning. If said admin isn't unblocked within 24 hours we will remove you from the group. 9. We do not allow any go fund me, donations or voting contests. 10. Posts must be about huskies only. 11. No breeding/stud/puppy selling posts are allowed in this group. Please leave those to your local Facebook pages. 12. We as an admin team do not recommend the furminator blade usage on our breed as it actually cuts the guard hairs and ruins the coats. Any comments recommending the blade will be deleted. If at anytime you have any issues, please contact one of the admins! Admins: Ashley Murphy Kailey Jordan Darr Deanna Marie Roper Kimberly Sue Harrison Shanna O’Leary Alicia Maxey Drake Troups Mods: Allyson Nice Jennifer Marie Karina Neuharth Sydney Beckers Tai Silver Trista Ammerman Brittany Ballard Ana Brock Have fun and lets see those fluff butts!

                 Golden Retrievers Lovers &amp; Owners
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group for people who love Golden Retrievers (and all animals - we just focus on Golden Retrievers here). Anyone spamming/scamming/attacking other posters may be removed without notice. If you feel a topic that is posted has bad or harmful content in it, REPORT the post to the Admins to be evaluated - DO NOT jump in to the topic and start attacking the poster or others as this may get you BANNED. Members of this group are INTERNATIONAL in nature - please keep that in mind. Please read the group sticky on our policy for attacking other posters in the group. If you do not like certain posts, we advise you use the "I don't want to see this" feature on Facebook to block the posting or the user - then you will no longer be subject to that topic or person's posts here. As always, you have the right to your own opinions, but you do not always have to share them, in particular in ways that are negative, nasty, or outright hateful. Intolerant or hateful posts based on Religious, political, ethnic or other forms of hate will be removed and the poster will be banned. Essentially, if you have nothing nice to say in a post or about another person posting, just don't say it :) If you think your dog has a medical problem, take them to your Vet and get a professional answer. While some of the people that frequent this page are professionals, you don't know any of them from a stranger living on the moon. Some people THINK they are professionals and give out medical advice as well. So please, rather than put your animal at risk, always consult your Vet in matters of anything health related to your dog or pet. People posting Rescue notices for Goldens - PLEASE try to verify there are not other postings for the same rescue on the page before you post yet another one. Use the "Search this group" box at the top of the page under the banner, and search for things like the shelter ID number for the animal. Again, please do not spam postings, additional posts may be removed. There is no advertising for products allowed. In the past we allowed it, but it got out of hand as the group enlarged. Do not spam postings for products - additional advertisements may be removed.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 BYC (BackYardChickens)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to BYC! We are a group dedicated to the discussion of backyard chickens &amp; other fowl for the purposes of eggs, meat, pets, show and exhibition, therapy animals, &amp; more. We are directly affiliated with the www.BackYardChickens.com website, PLEASE NOTE: Facebook provides very limited group discussion &amp; moderation tools and features. For a much better &amp; feature-rich experience, we STRONGLY suggest you visit and register (FREE) with www.BackYardChickens.com/forums Group Rules and Guidelines: •BYC is not a buy/sell/trade, ISO, or rehoming group. Please utilize the BYC forum for this purpose: backyardchickens.com/f/67/buy-sell-trade •BYC is an all-ages group. Posts containing profanity, innuendo, or other material that may be inappropriate for minors will be removed without warning. •Members may not use BYC to promote businesses, products, pages, groups, blogs, or other outside entities. •Political, religious, or inflammatory posts are not permitted and will be removed. •Discussion, encouragement, or suggestion of illegal behavior is strictly prohibited. (As according to US Federal law) •BYC welcomes both pet chicken owners, and those who raise their birds for eggs or meat. Discussion of animal processing will be a part of the conversation, and photos of the butchering process, necropsies, injuries, etc. are permitted. Such content may appear in this feed without graphic content warnings. •Photos of dead predators or of chickens who have been killed by predators should be posted in the comments with a "Graphic Content" warning in the original post. •We welcome discussions about all varieties of backyard fowl, including chickens, turkeys, ducks, guineas, peafowl, etc. Off-topic posts, including those about non-fowl livestock or pets, will be closed or removed without warning. For discussion about other animals: https://www.backyardchickens.com/forums/other-pets-livestock.22/ For off-topic discussion: backyardchickens.com/forums/random-ramblings.7/ •Comments should be constructive and relevant to the original post. Comments that are found to be abusive, derisive, or needlessly hostile will be removed, per the admin or moderators' discretion. -Failure or inability to abide by the rules and guidelines may result in a temporary mute, closed comments, deleted posts/comments, removal from the group, or a permanent ban at the discretion of the staff.-- ~REPORT A POST OR COMMENT Click or tap the drop-down menu for the post and select "report to admin". ~CONTACT A MOD/ADMIN For issues with group moderation, rules, etc., please email support@backyardchickens.com and provide as much detail, information, screenshots, etc. as possible. BYC TOS: backyardchickens.com/a/terms-of-service Website: www.backyardchickens.com BYC Page: facebook.com/raisingbackyardchickens

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Horse Health Discussion
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! Horse Health Discussion is a forum for mature and courteous individuals to seek opinions and information from other horse owners, professionals, and enthusiasts in regards to health, husbandry, nutrition, and hoof care - just like you would in your barn hallway! Advice and opinions expressed by members of this group solely reflect the individual; and Horse Health Discussions makes no claims to the validity or safety of any information. Advice and comments shall in no way replace the counsel of licensed professionals. Please note: Membership application submission should prompt questions to answer. Applications submitted without answered questions will be denied. We uphold a zero tolerance policy for inappropriate member conduct and any member found in violation at any time is subject to removal without warning. At no time is it acceptable to resort to personal attacks, sarcasm, trolling, or harassment publicly or via private message to our members. While we welcome personal recommendations of specific products, we do not allow any personal advertising for products, services, or events members may offer. Members may state if they are an equine professional in their field, but are not allowed to use this exception as a means to promote themselves. For example, in a discussion about navicular syndrome, a professional farrier may state they are a professional farrier and recommend the poster pursue XYZ method to resolve, but a professional farrier may NOT state they are a professional farrier and place a link to their website, phone number, or product they personally sell. All posts must be asking a specific, horse related question, or be worded to invite civil discussion in order to be approved. Please see the pinned post for suggestions on what information to include when submitting different types of questions. We are glad you have found us and look forward to your contribution to our ever expanding group! 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 &lt;3 Cats Make Me Happy, You Not So Much &lt;3 Welcome to all new members of the group! We have some little rules because we want a nice and peaceful group with lots of space for pictures and videos of our lovely cats and to share good information about the breed and health issues. • If you are a new member please introduce yourself and your cats off course. • This is an international group, so write English please. • Non active members will be removed. • Please do not advertise cats for sale • Please do not advertise merchandise;this is not a selling page • Please keep all comments respectful and not derogatory towards cats • Please do not criticize others over their choice of cat parenting styles • Please do not share any animal abuse pictures or videos • Please do not bully others or use any abusive language • Please no Gofundme posts allowed • Please do not post political opinions • Please do not share other people's posts without permission • Please note advice offered by members is not intended to be a substitute for professional veterinarian advice. • We do approve posts of kitties that are no longer with us. We as a group help members through the very difficult and sad time of losing their beloved fur babies by allowing the sharing of pictures and stories to celebrate their kitties lives. All posts are moderated daily and anything that does not comply with the group rules will be removed. [N.B.: Feel free to invite your all Cat Lovers friend to our group] *** Don't forget to like your page: www.fb.com/catsmakemehappy.org *** Thanks

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Saltwater Aquarium &amp; Reef Keepers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello and thanks for being a part of the Saltwater Aquarium &amp; Reef Keepers Community! We want this to be a supportive and friendly group so please follow the following guidelines when commenting or posting in the group. Failure to follow these guidelines may result in your comment or post being removed and you may also be muted for a period of time or removed from the group. We do not have time to send out individual reminders/warnings so please consider this your warning. 1) Stay on topic. This is not a place for Politics, Religion, Sports, Sexually suggestive/Explicit comments, Threats, Posting from profiles or PM's, Spam, or Trolling. 2) Be polite. Divisive, condescending, rude, insulting, etc. comments and posts are not allowed. 3) English Only Please This is so the admins can properly manage the group. 4) Check the links in announcements before posting There are a lot of the same post being posted over and over again; mostly for common pest &amp; hitchhiker ID's. If you post something that can be answered here it will be deleted as we would prefer you check here first to help control multiple post burying other posts. On this note the time to research is BEFORE you buy. 5) Buyers &amp; Sellers beware. If you are buying/trading with members on the group take time to research what you are buying to make sure it is what you really want. We cannot be responsible for deals gone bad. When in doubt maybe don’t do the deal. 6) No Drama You are expected to act civilly and like an adult. Please do so. No posting of screen captures from other groups here and vice versa, no posting of other groups here (unless it is a local reef group), no asking for votes in competitions, no posting of auctions, giveaways, or raffles (unless admin approved) 7) No "Tang Police" Posts or Comments Yes, for real. It's not original, it's not constructive, and it can encourage poor husbandry. If you have a tank that is smaller than recommended for the fish you want you can expect to be educated and you shouldn't let this offend you. Please use the following guidelines for group member interactions: If someone else bothers you: Block them (unless it’s an admin, sorry cannot allow blocking of any admin) If they say something you think violates FB rules: Report them to an Admin and/or block them If they post spam: Report the account &amp; report the post to admin If someone is being inappropriate: Report the post to admin Again, we strive to keep this group as friendly and as spam and drama free as possible. Your help with reporting spam and offensive content helps tremendously! Thanks again for helping make this the best Saltwater Aquarium and Reef Keeping group on Facebook!
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 All About Squirrels - * MODERATED *
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a Moderated group dedicated to the love and appreciation for Squirrels and their cousins in the Sciuridae family. Please be sure to answer the 3 questions and accept the group rules while joining, it helps us keep this group free of distractions, bots and trolls. Besides having fun, this is the entire point of having a moderated group. Not answering the questions will result in an immediate "NO" in response to your request to join. You are welcome to apply again but you need to complete the process. It's a simple requirement of this group. We need to know you're real. This is a moderated group, meaning that someone is paying attention at all times. Why we do this is very easy to explain: We want a safe, fun place for our members to share their appreciation for and knowledge of Squirrels and all members of the Family Sciuridae, the occasional racketycoon, bunnies and possies are always welcome 'cause they're all great. The purpose of this group is to share photos and stories and to learn more from each other as well as help educate others about these precious little creatures and all they do for us in the world. Simply put, "All About Squirrels - Moderated" is a squirrel appreciation group. That is it's only purpose. That will not change. We have ZERO tolerance for ANY DISRESPECT TOWARDS OTHER MEMBERS, trolling and etc. There will be no disrespect, hostility, bullying, name calling, endless debates with no point and individuals trying to ruin what we have created here. If you've been on Facebook for more than two weeks you have already seen it. C'mon, just no bickering and bullshit, too many other places for that elsewhere. This group was started by the moderators that have a love and appreciation for Squirrels after a similar page started experiencing things that group members found uncomfortable, disturbing and / or unpleasant. Such things included photos depicting harm or injury to squirrels or any animal, pro-hunting, trapping, Squirrel Helper Meme's (If you've seen it, I have a particular dislike for that meme) etc. Please don't bring it here, my humour does not run along those lines. IMPORTANT: We are not an emergency rescue group. If along the way we get the chance to help you or answer questions regarding the care and feeding of our little buddies, we encourage that in our group. If you've come looking for an emergency rescue, there are not people monitoring this group 24/7 for that type of post. We are privileged to have many seasoned and experienced rehabbers here. If you need help, please reach out to us and we will try and get someone to help ASAP, there are plenty of rehabber groups and the smaller the number the better the focus. Please see this site for Immediate Emergency Help in your area: https://ahnow.org/ Squirrel Rehabbers are a very caring, special type of human being, please give them the most respect possible, they certainly deserve it! Thank you! Sincerely, Doug and Joyce Your Group Admins
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Cats on Catnip Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is based on the Facebook page Cats on Catnip. Every purchase made in our store helps cats in rescue shelters by giving them 5 meals per purchase. We only support no-kill animal shelters that are dedicated to finding a furr-ever home for kitties ----&gt; www.catsoncatnip.co From time to time, your photos or videos may be featured on the official Cats on Catnip Facebook page! Please Note: Anyone not following the rules will be muted or removed. No warning will be issued. GROUP RULES 1. POST CAT RELATED THINGS ONLY. Post about a cat that you own, or start a positive discussion that is cat-related. 2. BE POSITIVE. Start conversations for the purpose of being positive, and being kind to people on a thread. There is to be no triggering content which may include death, abuse, suicide, self harm, hospital visits, break ups, life stories, sad posts etc. Complaining about admin, the page, group or other members will not be accepted. There is no judging, being rude, naming &amp; shaming, or swearing at others. Content depicting animals or humans that are injured, in distress, about to be put down, or deceased are not allowed. Posting a tribute to your cat that has passed is allowed, if it is not distasteful. Comments on tribute posts will be turned off after a minimum of 2 hours. 3. POSTING. Do not post your own site, business or group.This includes (but is not limited to) YouTube, Facebook pages/groups/profiles, Instagram, voting and donating. If you would like a donation plea to be submitted to our website, please email meow@catsoncatnip.co with the donation link, five HD images and your story in 600 unique words. This will not be posted in group but will be posted on our Facebook page to help you, and not within the group. 4. NO DEBATES. This means not inciting arguments by creating touchy polls or rants or asking questions that could cause problems in group by talking about controversial food eaten by cats, or objects used by cats. 5. NO SELLING. We cannot guarantee the authenticity of sellers, so there is to be no selling of any products or animals. This means cats or kittens cannot be advertised in the group for a cash amount, trade/swap or given away for free whether they are yours, a friends, or a random cat you have heard about. 6. NO RELIGIOUS/POLITICAL REFERENCES OR RACISM 7. NO BLOCKING ADMIN/MODERATORS If you block an admin or moderator, you will be banned. 8. MEDICAL QUESTIONS – You are welcome to ask the group ONLY for behavioural advice about your cat. If your question is medically related, please go to your local vet for a check-up. 9. NO MISSING PETS If you have an issue with someone’s comment or post, simply click on the top right and click ‘Report to admin’. Do not DM admins and moderators. If you must send a private message, please message the official Cats on Catnip page.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Doodles and Poodles Rescue and Adoption Network
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Our mission is to provide an place where people can rescue, adopt, rehome and network poodles and doodles every type you can imagine. We are NOT a rescue. We are a community that works together to unite loving homes with needy poos and doods through posts. We expect you to give as much as you get. Everyone is free to post dogs from shelters, Craigslist ads, and rescues or their own dog in need of a new home. Administrators and Moderators approve all posts, make sure you are posting with all needed information. We also love update posts when unions are made because of our group. This is not a place for breeders to sell their litter leftovers, we concentrate on rescue and re-home. Please read our rules and answer all questions or you will not be approved. We rarely post ISO's, we have a special register for that in our announcements, so you can be tagged. After you are approved, please go to announcements and read them thoroughly, so you know how to post things that will be approved and how to respond to posts. If there are any violation of rules in comments or posts, please report to a moderator or administrator. We have zero tolerance for breaking rules , for the sake of the dogs and the page.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Catspotting
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Catspotting Rules &amp; Guidelines (January 2020) Check out our Instagram page for features! @officialcatspotting Please read before you make your first post 😺 Catspotting is the game of ‘spotting’ a random cat and posting it in this group. Members may then award points to give the ‘spot’ a score. A spotted cat IS: - Unknown to you prior to the spot - Found unexpectedly - Real and alive - Accompanied by some context (who, what, when, where, how) A spotted cat is NOT: - Your own - A friends' or relatives' - Found on the internet - At a cat/animal oriented business (vet, cat cafe, pet store, shelter) Catspotting is NOT the place for: - Self-promotion or advertising - Fundraising pages - Seeking medical advice - Expletives - Fighting - Slurs - Gore or graphic content - Kitler jokes - Harassment - Homophobia - Racism - Sexism - Transphobia - Ableism - General rudeness - Non-cat spots - Spam What do you mean by CONTEXT? Context is the story/caption added to your post that shares the circumstances surrounding your spot. (Psssssst: the secret word is KIBBLE) Context may include: - What: what were you doing when you saw the cat? - When: when did you see the cat? Today, last week, last year, four years ago? - Where: where did you see/meet the cat? Examples: ‘Spotted this stranger while walking to the St. Paddy's Parade in Denver. He was chilling in a house along the way!’ ‘I walked past the bookshop in my hometown and saw these fresh-faced cuties in the window. I've lived here my whole life and only saw them today!’ You will be warned if your post does not include enough context. If context is still not provided, your post may be deleted without warning! Admin reserve the right to delete posts and ban members as they see fit. Have fun and happy spotting! 🐱
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Southern California Cat and Kitten Rescue Network 2.0
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! PLEASE READ what this page is about and adhere to our very basic rules: THE FOCUS OF THIS GROUP IS TO SAVE CATS &amp; KITTENS via rescue, fostering, re-homing, adoptions, etc. in Los Angeles, Orange, Riverside, San Bernardino, San Diego, Kern, Ventura and Imperial Counties, ETC. Please limit your posts to cats/kittens in these areas (not dogs, etc); avoid random “cute” videos/photos, and stay focused. Commercial products/services, including listing cats for sale by individuals, cannot be advertised here (a re-homing/adoption fee is OK). ALL POSTS &amp; REACTIONS MUST BE POSITIVE! Posts with negative words, hostile, and deliberately provocative posts will be removed and repeat offenders banned; inappropriate/offensive posts will be deleted without warning. Commercial products cannot be 'bashed' unless you can cite a valid scientific study indicating the commercial product is harmful or ineffective. Your personal experience on one animal does not constitute a rigorous study. Persons who continue to violate this rule will be banned from the group. This group focuses on the needs of shelter and street cats who need rescue. We aren't a platform to raise money for personal causes or pets who already have a home. Please refrain from religious or political references of any kind. Posts with religious or political content will be deleted. Continued violation will result in removal from the group. This group was created to provide an inclusive space for all individuals, regardless of their background or language preference. No xenophobia of any kind will be tolerated. Thank You.
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Aquarium Keepers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome everyone to Aquarium Keepers! We are an aquatic group that strives to cover all aspects of the hobby, being plants, tropicals, marines &amp; everything in between! Aquarium Keepers welcomes everyone who wants to share or expand their knowledge, ask questions or simply show off their fish. Whether a beginner, expert, breeder or hobbyist. We are a community based around the aquarium hobby, which means we allow fun posts and occasional off topic content to get to know one another better &amp; have fun! All rules and information can be found in the appropriate sections, and also in the announcement section of the group when you join. Please be sure to check them out. We encourage healthy, respectful debate &amp; sharing your experiences as we can all learn from each other! We hope you enjoy the group and love sharing your aquarium &amp; the hobby as much as we do. Again, welcome &amp; have fun! Head Admin: Jenny Price. Please get in touch for any questions / enquiries.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Rabbit Lovers ❤🐰
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the group "Rabbit Lovers❤🐰 PLEASE READ THE FOLLOWING! this group is for both pet owners/rabbit breeders *RULES!* 1. NO BULLYING!!!!! -Please respect eachother, if you can't you will have to find a different group to be in. We can all be mature. 2. ANYTHING POSTED ON HERE THAT IS CONSIDERED ANIMAL ABUSE WILL BE DELETED AND YOU WILL BE REMOVED! No warnings will be sent out. 3. We allow responsible rabbit breeders in the group please do not be rude towards them. We also allow people who keep their rabbits on wire flooring to be able to post. You may inform them if the picture/video does not show somewhere for them to get off the wire flooring but Don't assume they don't have one. if the wire flooring is not in good shape or the got gauges are too big please also inform them but be nice about it. 4. DO NOT GIVE FALSE INFORMATION THAT YOU KNOW ISN'T TRUE!! 5. DO NOT BLOCK AN ADMIN OR MODERATOR!! -doing so will get you removed 6. DO NOT POST FOR SALE POSTS ON HERE!!! -we aren't a sale group and there is many of them you can join to sell rabbits, this is a group to post pictures of your rabbits and share the love for them. 7. ANYTHING NOT RELATED TO RABBITS WILL BE DELETED! 8. No advertisements of anything(group/page/GoFundMe and other) unless it is On Fridays and an admin/mods will make posts for that. 9. DO NOT JOIN JUST TO ADVERTISE STUFF, THIS IS NOT A GROUP TO ADVERTISE. ITS A GROUP TO ENJOY TALKING AND POSTING ABOUT RABBITS. 10. DON’T ARGUE WITH AN ADMIN. - If an admin tells you to stop doing something, stop, or leave the group. 11. If you don't answer the questions or are not in common groups of the admins you will not be accepted. - We have had too many accepted in the group and not follow the rules -Please remember new rabbit owners join/post in this group, we are here to help better their knowledge of rabbits needs WE are trying to be a DRAMA FREE group. -Don't use aggressive language -Don't be rude to someone who is trying to help you. - If we can't do that we will turn off comments or delete the post. rules are not hard to follow. This Group was made for everyone who has or likes rabbits. Post about your rabbit/s pictures are welcomed of course! If you have any questions you can ask them here! If you have a concern or complaint about a member in this group please message an Admin! If there is a post that isn't following the rules or is childish please report it to Admin or tag an admin. IF THESE RULES ARE NOT FOLLOWED YOU WILL GET A WARNING if you continue to break the rules you are out rules are pretty simple to follow. Our Admin team - Shaylynne Hamilton (MO, USA) Josiah Gelatt (KS, USA) Isabella Ferritto (Ontario, Canada) Samantha Shafer (USA) Breanna Lynn (USA) Danielle Chartier (USA) Laura Margaret Foley (USA) Our mod team - Piper McAllister Karen Merlos LASTLY, HAVE FUN!!!! if you have any questions don't be scared to ask. admin question wise or rabbit question wise. 😃
